评论人：omarakkad
评论时间：2018-02-11
评论内容：L’uomo sul treno di Jaume Collet-Serra Un film d’azione, per certi versi classico, le cui caratteristiche rientrano pienamente nel filone di film d’azione. Il protagonista è il solito uomo, arrivato per certi versi al limite (con l’età e le sue vicissitudini private), dalla moralità inflessibile e con capacità fuori dal normale, che si ritrova a dover salvare le vite dei passeggeri di un treno. Per certi versi dunque è un film classico senza grosse sorprese, qualche caratteristica leggermente curiosa, però, la troviamo: una fotografia ben curata con inquadrature di primi piani e di particolari molto ben fatte e la presenza di una regia che prova tramite qualche trucchetto e stratagemma a farsi un po’ furba. Lo sviluppo della trama è molto ordinato e procede in modo lineare e semplice per gran parte del film , così come il treno in questione, fino a poco prima del finale dove sia il racconto, che il treno, escono un po’ dai binari per un finale abbastanza originale. Una nota negativa personalmente l’ho trovata nelle scene d’azione, in cui si nota che Liam Neeson non è più un giovanotto e sente il bisogno di usare la CGI per certi combattimenti, cosa che rende le scene meno scorrevoli e fluide. In conclusione quindi un film d’azione carino che riesce a intrattenere senza alcun problema. Voto personale: 6 #luomosultreno #liamneeson #thecommuter #film #movies #recensioni #recensionifilm #cinema

评论人：moviemadness97
评论时间：2018-02-11
评论内容：The Commuter (2018) - 6/10 I really enjoyed this movie. Yeah its a over the top action movie but look this is what i want in a Liam Neeson action movie. It is like alot of Neeson’s other movies but its a movie you can just sit and enjoy and leave your worries behind. So you guessed this movie takes place on a train and with that you have a unique root you can take with the plot. Not quite sure why i enjoy movies that take place on a train ? Like i loved Murder on the Orient Express and then i really enjoyed this. The fighting scenes in this were surprisingly well editing and choreographed. Neeson can kick ass as usual. I like that Liam Neeson is trying to recreate a famous 80s movie ... first we had him in a Plane in Non-Stop, then we see him in this movie on a Train so I’m guessing we are going to see him in a movie where its set in a car. If you don’t get what I’m saying is the Liam Neeson is recreating Planes, Trains and Auto-mobiles. Overall its a really fun action flick that you don’t need to take seriously but its fun to watch. It stars Liam Neeson, Vera Farmiga, Patrick Wilson, Jonathan Banks, Elizabeth McGovern and Sam Neill. Its about insurance salesman Michael who is on his daily commute home, which quickly becomes anything but routine. After being contacted by a mysterious stranger, Michael is forced to uncover the identity of a hidden passenger on the train before the last stop. As he works against the clock to solve the puzzle, he realizes a deadly plan is unfolding, and he is unwittingly caught up in a criminal conspiracy that carries life and death stakes for everyone on the train. #thecommuter #movie #cinema #moviereview #moviemadness6

评论人：themoviehouse02
评论时间：2018-02-11
评论内容：My first review! 'The Commuter' was the first movie I saw in 2018, and I'll therefore review it first. The premise of the movie, despite being a concurring premise, is pretty interesting. The plot is pretty good and driven by Michael's (Liam Neeson) love for his family. What I don't like about the story is that the movie ends, and there is still some mystery and unanswered questions. Vera Farmiga's character feels purposeless at the end of the movie and questions surrounding her remain untouched, which leaves her being a weak character. The action is fine for the most part but sometimes the way it's shot feels too extra in such a narrow area which is a train. In fact, the best parts are when Michael investigates subtly, rather than when he engages in action. During his investigations, the main character makes some rather questionable decisions that make you wonder where exactly he's trying to reach. The performances are good, and Liam Neeson stands out as usual. Overall, The Commuter is an enjoyable movie but feels like there's a bit more left to see by the end. Rating: 68% (D+) #movie #movies #film #films #theater #cinema #thecommuter #thecommutermovie #2018 #liamneeson #verafarmiga #themovie #themoviehousereviews

评论内容：Finalmente, sono riuscita a vedere L'uomo sul treno e mi è piaciuto moltissimo! Genere thriller, con un Liam Neeson un pò meno giovane, ma intenso e carismatico anche nei panni di un prevedibile assicuratore, che fa il pendolare 😊. La trama del film è incentrata su lui e sul treno, ovviamente. Il titolo originale è "The Commuter", il pendolare, probabilmente chi ha tradotto il titolo, lo ha trovato un pò troppo minimalista e ha preferito "L'uomo sul treno", che a me non piace; considerando, che abbiamo appena visto "La ragazza del treno". Comunque il film non ha nulla in comune con quest'ultimo. Michael McCauley, ovvero Liam Neeson, viene improvvisamente licenziato dalla compagnia di assicurazioni per la quale lavora da oltre dieci anni. Si sfoga al bar con un suo ex collega poliziotto e amico, Alex Murphy, con cui è stato in pattuglia per oltre sette anni. Poi, riprende, tristemente, la via del ritorno. La perdita del lavoro non era prevista, due mutui, un figlio da mandare al college e la loro situazione bancaria non rosea. Michael non riesce ad immaginare nessun modo per comunicarlo alla moglie e al figlio. Sul solito treno, più affollato di quelli italiani, i soliti visi, più qualcuno nuovo, tra cui una donna, Joanna, che si siede proprio di fronte a lui e incomincia a parlare: "Che tipo di persona è lei? Se io le chiedessi di fare una cosa piccola, la farebbe?" Da vedere!!! 👋#cinema #movie #guardolibrileggofilm #luomosultreno #thecommuter #film #thespacecinema #cinemachepassione #liamneeson #buonavisione #thriller #train #treno #lookingfor #mistery #greatactor #movie #buonaserata #carisma #action

评论人：david_marmolejo
评论时间：2018-02-08
评论内容：The Commuter “Next time, I’ll take the bus.” Juame Collet-Serra Every Liam Neeson film that is released, is bound to be a solid thriller. Nothing fancy, but entertaining, no matter what situation, you’ll root for Liam Neeson because of his skills. Also, because he’s a great actor, doing all with what he has to work with. From saving his family multiple times, to dealing with scenarios of life and death in puzzling fashion, on a plane and now on a train, it pretty much ends the same predictable way. The Commuter keeps you interested, you can guess the villain in less than five minutes of this film, but you’ll like to see it unfold. It’s Murder on the Orient Express in present time sort of. Worth a matinee or rental, hopes shouldn’t be high but it’s likable, just don’t expect much but a time killer. Clean sequences, ok cast, cheesy script, and Liam Neeson, that’s all anyone ever needs sometimes. #thecommuter #liamneeson #patrickwilson #verafarmiga #samneill #film #filmaddict #movie #movieaddict #thursday #particularsetofskills #juamecolletserra #thriller

评论人：it_reaches_the_soul
评论时间：2018-02-08
评论内容：We watched The Commuter in the #movietheater. There are a lot of people comparing this to Nonstop. I can see why, both are thrillers on forms of transportation starring #LiamNeeson, but #thecommuter has a better script and makes for a more enjoyable #movie. Neeson plays Michael, an ex cop that has been working as an insurance salesman for the last ten years. He rides the commuter train into #NewYork each day, but then he gets laid off. He gets some drinks with his old partner Alex Murphy (not Robocop 😂) played by #PatrickWilson. We also meet the police chief (#SamNeill), who Michael is surprised has risen that far. On his way home, a mysterious woman approaches him (#VeraFarmiga) and offers him $100K to find a person on the train. He’s desperate for money after losing his job and decides to play along. Little does he know what will happen once he finds the person. He begins to get an idea when he tries to call for help. People are killed and his family is in danger. It’s a good #thriller with some #mystery elements. The villains are very Machiavellian, but a huge corruption conspiracy is hinted and I like that we are kept mostly in the dark about it. It allows the villains motive to remain unknown. I also like that the #film subverts expectations on certain characters. It was solid and entertaining. ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️

评论人：4criticos
评论时间：2018-02-07
评论内容：Luego de realizar películas como “Non-stop” o “Desconocido”, Jaume Collet-Serra (director) y Liam Neeson (protagonista) se juntaron nuevamente para realizar otro thriller de acción. Y la fórmula sigue siendo más q satisfactoria. El film es muy ágil, atrapante y utiliza a la perfección la (prácticamente) única locación donde se desarrolla, un tren. Con escenas de acción en espacios reducidos, lo que favorece mucho a Neeson, y un guión que pese a algunos baches tiene buenos giros y sorpresas, “The commuter” consigue mantener al espectador enganchado hasta el final. Quizás la única mancha importante son algunas escenas exageradas e innecesarias sobre el final. Pero nada que una película de este género no pueda perdonar. Está claro que no hay novedad en la cinta. El tándem Collet-Serra/Neeson apela a una marca registrada en esta película. Pero haciendo esto no decepcionan. Al contrario, cumplen a la perfección la tarea de entretener. #4criticos #cine #cinema #peliculas #liamneeson #jaumecolletserra #thecommuter #elpasajero

评论人：cool_cash18
评论时间：2018-02-06
评论内容：The Commuter (2018) Movie Review! 🚊 ________________________ Directed by: Jaume Collet-Serra ________________________ Plot: A businessman on his daily commute home gets unwittingly caught up in a criminal conspiracy that threatens not only his life but the lives of those around him. ________________________ Review: The first movie released in 2018 reviewed!!! The Commuter is another paired effort between Liam Neeson and director Jaume Collet-Serra. I really liked their airplane movie “Non-Stop”, and The Commuter is almost the same plot but on a train and Neeson’s character is more vulnerable. Let’s start with the positives. Liam Neeson is great once again here, chipping in a splendid performance and doing well in the action sequences. He may be getting old, but he can still pack many punches. The action is filmed quite nicely, not a lot of shaky cam and relying more on the emotional weight. You feel the punches and kicks thrown onboard the train. I also liked the sense of less atmosphere on the train, since it is an enclosed location. The camerawork and cinematography are great. Coming to the performances, I felt everyone else did serviceable. Patrick Wilson was fine, Vera Farmiga seemed wasted and a little off-key with her boring character, and Sam Neill was decent as the lead officer. Of course Neeson is worth making this movie enjoyable. The movie knows what it is, a simple thriller with a somewhat convoluted plot sadly. It’s never fully explained why Liam Nelson’s character is brought onto this mission. Into the negatives. There’s some really bad CGI in the nighttime sequences when the train crashes. The third act suffers with predictability to the villain, and the slow pacing can be felt. Overall, I felt The Commuter was a fine action movie, light on character development and stronger on entertainment value. ________________________ Verdict: ⭐️⭐️⭐️ #thecommuter #liamneeson #moviereview #movie #filmreview #film #theconjuring

评论人：the_cynic_critic
评论时间：2018-02-05
评论内容：My review of “The Commuter”- Going into this movie, my expectations weren’t too high. Working at my job for several hours prior, I was psychically and mentally exhausted, and I simply wanted to watch a fun movie that wouldn’t require me to use my brain too hard. With this in mind, “The Commuter” is exactly the kind of movie I wanted it to be, for better and (occasionally) for worse. Featuring frequent collaborators Liam Neeson and director Jaume Collet-Serra, this action flick is about a man named Michael who gets caught up in a criminal conspiracy while on a train after accepting a job that is given to him by a fellow passenger. Michael (played by Liam Neeson) is a pretty normal and unremarkable guy, with the films great opening segment showing just how repetitive (yet still enjoyable) his life his. Unfortunately, his life comes crashing down once he is inexplicably fired from his job, and he heads back home, sad and ashamed, on the train he has been on almost every day for the past ten years. Joanna (played by Vera Farmiga) is aware of Michael’s familiarity with the train and his recent firing, and uses these facts to give Michael an offer he can’t resist; for 100,000 dollars, he has too simply find someone on the train whom he feels doesn't belong. As Michael accepts the task, the movie kicks into gear. For a significant chunk of the movie, the pacing is swift and snappy, and I was captivated by the chaos that was taking place. Liam Neeson is to be thanked for my captivation, for he helps make Michael a very relatable and sympathetic character, which in turn makes one heavily invested in the fire journey he takes. Thankfully, this journey is well directed by Jaume Collet-Serra, who makes the action sequences very fun to look at and successfully allows the tension to pile onto itself. One fight in particular (involving an ax) had me on the edge of my seat as the fight neared its intense conclusion. Unfortunately, while this particular fight scene has a satisfying conclusion, the same can’t be said for the movie as a whole. (Continued in the comments section)

评论人：hesaidshesaidmoviereviews
评论时间：2018-02-05
评论内容：THE COMMUTER HE SAID: Have you seen the film Non Stop in which Liam Neeson plays a grizzled, Irish American lawman who receives a mysterious phone call and is challenged to find a mysterious passenger to prevent everyone from dying on the flight he is on? Yeah I’ve seen it too and I just rewatched the exact same film only this time it’s on a train and it’s called The Commuter! And here’s the thing - I enjoyed it...again! Taken was terrible (I didn’t bother watching 2 & 3) but it gave Neeson a new lease of life as an ageing action star and for the most part, his B-movie action films with this director have all been surprisingly enjoyable. This film also includes the best fight on a train since Sean Connery and Robert Shaw in From Russia With Love. One thing that’s really lacking in today’s cinematic climate is the mid budget action/thrillers of the 80’s and 90’s - where are your buddy cop movies? Your psychosexual drama? Your John Grisham adaptations? Your ticking clock suspense movies? Of late this is about as close as we’ve gotten to a straight up, fun B-movie and I’ll take(n) it. Instantly forgettable but fun all the same. SHE SAID: Imagine playing Cluedo with Agatha Christie on a train and Liam Neeson is your board piece: that’s The Commuter! The film opens with a sleek montage of mornings, giving depth to Neeson’s cop-turned-insurance broker backstory. His life immediately feels real, and we are ready to believe that he could and would wind up in one hell of an afternoon commute. Neeson is often an oxymoron: strong in stature but soft in manner. Here is a prime example, as he tries to locate a mysterious passenger while being framed as a hijacker who has seen Falling Down one too many times. We believe that he could beat a man using an electric guitar and that he could look like a nice guy while doing it. The Commuter is, to be fair, Non-stop on train tracks. And I’m ok with that. Next up, I hope Neeson and director Jaume Collet-Serra do a murder mystery on a cruise ship. They could call it Taken on Board!

评论人：cinefilexterian
评论时间：2018-02-04
评论内容："Todo comienza como cualquier trama de intriga, en la que sabes que las cosas no van a salir bien para nuestro desgraciado protagonista, y a medida que van pasando los minutos, esa intriga va cogiendo forma en tu estómago y en tu cabeza, creándose unas ilusiones, que van perdiendo un poco de fuelle, para aquellos impacientes adictos al caos y la acción empedernida, que no pueden pasar ni unos fugaces y necesarios “tranquilos” minutos, contemplando como lo mejor, está por llegar. Y llega cuando menos te lo esperas. Te pega un bofetada en la cara sin darte cuenta, dejándote sin respiración y las pulsaciones a mil, mientras contemplas escenas de infarto, en las que te tienes que agarrar a ti mismo o al desconocido del asiento del al lado, por miedo a salir disparado contra la butaca de atrás, si te alcanza alguna patada o bala perdida, en una trama que se mantiene intacta y sosegada, hasta que aumenta y estalla en mil pedazos, de brillante, y pura maestría cinematográfica. Jaume Collet-Serra, es un director, que sabe hacer películas, para toda clase de público, que lo que desea de verdad, es pasarlo verdaderamente mal, dejando de lado el género del drama, que ya se está repitiendo demasiadas veces, y que parece ser el único merecedor, de una inútil y clasicista estatuilla de oro. Jame Collet-Serra nos deja ver una vez más, que los espacios reducidos como un avión o un tren, son el escenario perfecto para desarrollar una trama explosiva, embaucadora y sobresaliente, que no deja a ningún espectador insatisfecho. Al contrario, nos sorprende, nos intriga, nos engaña, nos manipula, y sobretodo, nos hace saltar por los aires, sin dejarnos un solo segundo para poder tomar aire, pensar en lo que está ocurriendo y en lo que puede ocurrir, y darnos la mínima oportunidad para acomodarnos y poder detener ese tic nervioso que hace acelerar aún mas, nuestra tensión, que se va esparciendo por todos los capilares de nuestra piel." 评论人：moviereviews7
评论时间：2018-02-04
评论内容：The Commuter ~ PG-13 ~ 2018 ~ #JaumeColletSerra #LiamNeeson #VeraFarmiga #PatrickWilson #JonathanBanks #SamNeill #ColinMcFarlane After being laid off, a financially struggling businessman is offered the opportunity to find a specific person that doesn’t belong on his daily commuter train for a large amount of money. Okay, so I actually enjoyed this movie a lot more than I thought I would. Liam Neeson has had this stereotype ever since Taken where he plays yet another badass old guy in a mediocre, forgettable action movie. While The Commuter might still fall under that category, it definitely exceeded my expectations. Don’t get me wrong, there still are a fair amount of notable flaws. Character development was kept to a minimum, the acting was all relatively poor, & the third act is littered with an absurd amount of illogical writing. Regardless, this movie did what it’s main goal was: to entertain. As little invested as I was in the characters, the story remains consistent & fails to have a dull moment. The movie never takes itself too seriously, so I never really felt like the film was failing to do what it was trying to. I enjoyed the multiple scenarios Neeson’s character put himself in & even when the third act got a little over-the-top, I was still having fun. Would I ever watch this again on my own? Probably not. But I definitely didn’t find it to be the slightest of chores to watch this cheap thriller. 3/5 #TheCommuter #train #passenger #passengertrain #commuter #action #mystery #thriller #movie #film #moviereview

评论人：reviews_by_dean
评论时间：2018-02-04
评论内容：The Commuter is a movie starring Liam Neeson and directed by Jaume Collet-Sierra. The movie is about a man who is tasked by a woman to find a person with a certain bag going to a certain place and kill them. The movie is solid for the first two acts. It’s a nice action thriller with a race against the clock twist in an enclosed environment. It’s a fun movie, but with some odd “screw the upper-class” sentiments thrown in, but still solid. It brings good performances, and surprisingly good, but gimmicky direction. The third act, however goes completely off the rails, pardon my pun. It shifts the movie’s focus away from the interesting half mystery half action movie I was expecting, to a very overblown CGI mess. Without giving anything away, it almost shifts types of action movies to a completely different sub genre, and does some things that make no rational sense and may not even be possible. Another issue I have, is with the dialogue. It’s all very hokey and unrealistic. The attempts at comedy fall flat and the attempt at relating to the audience fails. All in all, it’s a perfectly passable movie, that is only accentuated by Jaume Collet-Sierra’s direction. #film #moviereview #movie #review #cinema #liamneeson #action #thriller #mystery #actionmovie #thecommuter #train

评论内容：[Movie Review] The Commuter (2018) #KataKinema . The Commuter stars Liam Neeson as Michael McCauley, an ex-insurance salesman who is confronted by a mysterious woman, named Joanna (Vera Farmiga), on his daily commute home. Little did he know that Joanna is bad news, now Michael is blackmailed into finding someone on the train, where not only the lives of his family are at stake, but also the lives of everyone on the train. . I like the action scenes, I think they are well shot and well choreographed. I also like the thrilling whodunit moments. What I dislike, however, is the movie is taking itself too seriously, while there a lot of implausibilities and a few plot holes. If it doesn’t take itself seriously, I think I might’ve ignored the flaws and enjoyed it a little more. In conclusion, this movie is an enjoyable and thrilling action movie, only when you don’t try to make sense out of it. But if you do, it turns into an enjoyable, mindless, silly, and thrilling action movie. . KinemaScore: 2.5 out of 5 . So, what do you guys think? Let us know in the comment section! . The Shape Of Water expanded further and got some good results but $50M worldwide isn't that great.

评论内容：THE COMMUTER CINERATE: 7 out of 10 CINEOPSYS Michael menghabiskan hari-harinya hidupnya di kereta utk perjalanan dr rmh ke tempat kerja. Hingga suatu hari, kedekatan hidupnya dengan dunia kereta sangat diperlukan utk memecahkan misteri yang membuat Michael, secara tidak langsung, terjebak dalam sebuah konspirasi kejahatan. CINENOTES Film ini sangat menonjolkan Liam Neeson sebagai tokoh protagonis. Sempitnya ruang geral di dalam kereta membuat semua aksi Liam Neeson terlihat maksimal. Untungnya, Liam memberikan performa terbaiknya untuk film ini. Awal film ini sangat artistik, sinematografi yang memukau terasa kira-kira sampai 20-25 menit pertama, selebihnya tidak ada efek visual yang sedinamis awalnya. Film ini memiliki logika filmnya sendiri, terutama bila mau mengupas logiks konspirasinya, sehingga cukup ditonton dengan menikmati setiap adegannya. Ada banyak kritik di dalamnya bila mau berpikir lebih keras, tapi sebuah pesan yang normatif. Kesimpulannya, film ini adalah sebuah cerita yang sederhana, dikemas dengan konspirasi yang pelik. 评论内容：. THE COMMUTER . Michael MacCauley (Liam Neeson) ist Versicherungsmakler und führt ein beschauliches Leben. Seit zehn Jahren pendelt er jeden Tag mit dem Zug aus dem verschlafenen Vorort, in dem er mit seiner Familie lebt, nach Manhattan. Doch eines Tages wird seine Routine gestört: Er trifft während der morgendlichen Zugfahrt auf eine mysteriöse Fremde namens Joanna (Vera Farmiga), die sich zu ihm setzt und ihn in ein Gespräch verwickelt. Nach und nach offenbart sie Michael, dass sie nicht einfach nur an Smalltalk interessiert ist. Wenn er mit Hilfe von zwei vagen Hinweisen einen bestimmten Passagier an Bord des Zuges findet, dann winkt ihm eine hohe Belohnung. Sollte er sich jedoch weigern, ist nicht nur das Leben aller Mitreisenden in Gefahr, sondern auch das von Michaels Familie. Ihm bleibt keine andere Wahl, als Joannas Spiel mitzuspielen - und er hat nur eine Stunde Zeit... . . #thecommuter #liamneeson . . #APOLLOundCENTRAL #apolloneheim #apolloarnsberg #neheim #arnsberg #sauerland #kinoneheim #nrw #bestepopcorn #kino #popcorn #film

评论人：the_honest_usher
评论时间：2018-01-31
评论内容：The Commuter Directed by: Jaume Collet-Serra Starring: Liam Neeson, Patrick Wilson, Vera Farmiga A man on his daily commute back home is approached by a stranger with a hypothetical preposition, and a reward that is not so hypothetical. The first thing of notice that makes this a clever and engaging ride is the editing and camerawork; films primarily set in one location can easily become repetitive and lack the ability to make the audience anticipate what will happen next. Here however the editing creates a quickened pace that moves the plot along and makes this film feel like its supposed to (a thriller). It also manages to convey visual story-telling in a way that is so effective it removes the need for exposition. The camerawork keeps the location from ever feeling too familiar, the varying use of close-ups and tracking wide shots are relevant to the mood of the protagonist; and this causes his motivations and inner conflicts to be easily displayed on-screen. Not that that would be an issue anyway, as Liam Neeson proves again that he is the best at playing an "everyday-man" who knows how to kick ass. The film has a strong cast, although most of the other actors and actresses feel like they are only in cameo roles next to Neeson, who to allow the narrative to work well, is mostly isolated for the majority of the film. The tension is well built and it comes from being able to easily draw empathy from Neeson's performance; that is his best since Taken. The narrative proceeds logically although it bares a lot of noticeable similarities to other films (many of which I can't mention because...spoilers) but despite this it manages to be better than the films it either draws inspiration from or is coincidentally parallel to. The only negative to be seen is the fact that Neeson's character appears to have John McClane syndrome, and can be put through a lot more physical trauma than what you would expect of a man of his age, it doesn't detract from the fun of watching Neeson in action again but it is rather prevalent, and does have an impact on the validity of the character. Overall, a fast and cleverly put-together train ride that gives plenty to think about. 9/10

评论人：framereel
评论时间：2018-01-31
评论内容：Next on the Liam Neeson's Transportation Conspiracy! THE COMMUTER Commuting isn't the most fertile source for interest when it comes to a movie, it's about a boring routine that you passionlessly do to get from point A to B. This film emulates all the thrills of commuting and resolves to meld them to an unnecessarily complicated plot. And, you know, it can be nice to take the train for the first time but once you've done it several times, it stops being refreshing. As so, if you see the same movie played out with slight differences over the course of a year, you lack that feeling of renewal - that's why John Wick's film are so appreciated, they bring something new. After having seen Non Stop and Run All Night, you can't help to be indifferent to the same actor-director combination, specially when the cuts, characters and plot feel the same, Jaume Collet-Serra's storyboard decisions feel the same and even the colour grading seems to gloom across all this transportation method trilogy. However, although it's completely uneventful, I didn't dislike The Commuter. There's a security in a commute like this where the elements are so played out that they are bound to work. Furthermore, there is one shot that is incredibly good and there is actual tension built around a premise, which many action films fail to do. It's like going to work in an office, it's a service and in this case, enough has been done to make it serviceable. It's incoherent but it has a lot of personal style, it's cookie-cutter but it is sufficiently well put together to make you actually care and feel some suspense for what's going to happen next. It's no Unstoppable or (for Hitchcock's sake) Strangers on a Train, but its main strength comes from the realization that the movie consists on seemingly one-trick pony of a star kicking ass in yet another mode of transport. #thecommuter #liamneeson #verafarmiga #filmreview #filmcritic

评论内容：Here's a list of all the new releases that I watched this month with my ratings. 1) Three billboards outside ebbing, Missouri - 9/10 I heard a lot of great things about this but I wasn't expecting to love it as much as I did. This was the first film I watched in 2018, and I expect it to be in my top 5 come the end of the year. Frances Mcdormand and Sam Rockwell were brilliant and I expect them both to win Oscars. ----------------------------- 2) Molly's game - 8/10 I didn't know anything about Molly Bloom going into this, and I think that made me enjoy the movie more because I didn't know how things ended up for her. Jessica Chastain was brilliant and really owned the movie - there isn't anyone who would have been better cast. ----------------------------- 3)Coco - 8/10 It's definitely up there with being one of the better Disney films. I didn't know a lot about the Day of the Dead but having seen this I feel like it's given me a whole new outlook on death - I thought the movie did a great job showing off the culture and tradition. ----------------------------- 4)The Commuter - 7/10 Liam Neeson on public transport fighting to keep his family alive. You knew exactly what you're going to get and it didn't disappoint. ----------------------------- 5) The Post - 7/10 I thought it was well made and had great performances from Meryl Streep and Tom Hanks. However I found the actual story to be quite boring in parts ----------------------------- 6) 12 Strong - 7/10 Although the actual true story is unbelievable, I thought the film fell short of capturing this. However I thought the action scenes were great and it had some good performances, showing that they were just normal men that were sent to fight. ----------------------------- 7) Hostiles 6/10 Again another one with decent performances, and when there was action it was quite intense. However when there wasn't any action it felt quite dull and dragged on a bit longer than it needed to be ----------------------------- 8) Early Man - 3/10 I knew this would be shit and it didn't fail at that, was full of stupid accents that were there to make little kids laugh. I'm not even sure if I like football anymore

评论人：fmcrreviews
评论时间：2018-01-29
评论内容：The Commuter (2018) - 6.7/10 • “What kind of a person are you?” “Insurance salesman Michael is on his daily commute home, which quickly becomes anything but routine. After being contacted by a mysterious stranger, Michael is forced to uncover the identity of a hidden passenger on the train before the last stop. As he works against the clock to solve the puzzle, he realizes a deadly plan is unfolding, and he is unwittingly caught up in a criminal conspiracy that carries life and death stakes for everyone on the train.” At the beginning it was really confusing and slow, then it started getting better and better, developing the character more and setting more challenges. The storyline felt sometimes weird and without an actual point. The action scenes were good but everything seemed unnecessary, or overly exaggerated. The plot was a little confusing but the actors did a good job portraying their characters. It is overall an ok crime movie with some plot holes and the final rating is a 6.7/10, recommended. • 👇🏽Comment your opinion below👇🏽 • #movie #film #cinema #review #thecommuter #critique #fmcr #trains #crime #mystery

Is he thinking just about himself or is he going to take into consideration the possible moral consequences of what he’s asked to do? That’s the question we want the audience to ask themselves.”

评论人：a_movie_critic
评论时间：2018-01-28
评论内容："The Commuter" was another thriller by Liam Neeson and it does not disappoint in the cinema, but when you're done with the movie, you kind of reflect back on the things that didn't make sense but did while you were watching it. First: thing: The Plot. I was very intrigued with the storyline but it did turn out a little bit unrealistic at the end. The mystery to the movie was acceptable but some parts were predictable and the person who did not belong on the train was not expected. Second: the cast and characters. Liam Neeson was pretty good in his role and Vera Farmiga was ok, so was Patrick Wilson. I did like how Jonathan Banks was in it because he was amazing in "Breaking Bad". Everyone else was average. Finally: the music and editing. The action scenes were not well done and the original score for the movie did not blend well with the whole suspense and plot. The editing is not really something to appreciate because (SPOILER) there is a scene where the train is moving sideways for a long amount of time and that is impossible. This movie wasn't a big success in reviews it it is a fan favorite now which is why I am going to rate this movie with a 62%. Thank you guys for reading my review and I'll see you next time. Bye! #the #commuter #thecommuter #liamneeson #verafarmiga #patrickwilson #jonathanbanks #mystery #thriller #action #movie #movienight #moviereview #review #moviecritic #critic #university #nyu #chapman #syracuse #loyola #lafi #amoviecritic

GV는 자주 다녔지만 큐레이터 프로그램은 처음이었는데 끝나고 해설을 들어보니 나름 고대 문학과도 연관이 많은 작품이었다는 걸 깨달았다. - <커뮤터> : 이제는 그냥 액션배우 리암 니슨의 액션 영화. 킬링타임으론 나쁘지 않다. 그런데 이제는 그의 액션 영화의 피로도가 누적되서인지 뭘 봐도 비슷해 보인다는 단점이 있다. 리암 니슨과 가족이 되면 일단 인질이 되는 건 기본 옵션일 듯. 이제 액션은 쉬세요..

评论内容：커뮤터 (무난함) 비행기랑 기차 탔으니까 이제 배 타는 일만 남은거죠? - CGV에서 븨아픠 회원들을 대상으로 진행했던 서프라이즈 티켓에 당첨돼서 <커뮤터>를 무료로 관람했다. 근데 뭐 딱히 할 말이 없는 전형적인 킬링타임 영화라고 할 수 있겠다. - 매일 같은 곳을 왕복하는 통근 기차에서 일어나는 일을 다루고 있는만큼 그것과 연결하여 만들어진 오프닝이 인상적으로 다가온다. 마이클이 매일 같은 시간에 일어나서 비슷한 일상을 살아가는 장면을 콜라주로 연결하여 보여주는 오프닝은 짧은 시간내에 그가 살고있는 환경과 가장으로서의 모습을 효과적으로 드러내준다. - 관객들은 철저하게 마이클의 시점으로 무슨 일이 일어나는지 모르는 상태로 상황에 접근하기 떄문에 몰입감은 상당히 뛰어나다. 누가 프린인지 가방에는 뭐가 들어있는지 그리고 도대체 무슨 일이 벌어지고 있는지 전혀 감을 잡을 수가 없다. 그렇게 승객들을 한명한명 의심하며 일이 진행되지만 이상하게 <오리엔트 특급 살인>와 비슷하게도 긴장감이 전혀 느껴지지 않았다. - 이미 <테이큰>과 <논스톱> 등등 여러 영화에서 비슷한 이미지의 캐릭터를 연기한 리암니슨이 또 같은 유형의 영화를 찍어야 할 이유가 있어야 했나싶다. 특히 60살 먹은 노인이면 액션은 좀 빼주자 인간적으로... 팔팔한 20~30대랑 싸움을 붙이다니... 리암 니슨이 맞는 모습을 볼 때마다 안타까움의 탄식이 나왔다. <논스톱>은 비행기에서 이야기를 다루고 <커뮤터>는 기차에서 이야기를 다루고 있으니까 다음에는 <크루즈>라고 해서 배 타는 이야기를 다루면 될 것 같다. 지긋지긋.. 보고 계시나요 감독님? #일상 #취미 #영화 #영화알못 #영화스타그램 #인스타무비 #무비스타그램 #movie #film #커뮤터 #TheCommuter #리암니슨

评论内容：MOVIE REVIEW: If you're willing to turn your brain off and enjoy yourself, #TheCommuter is a surprisingly good time. There is a lot more tension and excitement than we anticipated. Much of the action enters into over the top, "what the hell is physics?" territory, but let's face it, we don't seek out #LiamNeeson action films for their realism. The mystery has a little bit of intrigue, though it is not tightly put together and we never felt wowed by that aspect of it. The camerawork gets pretty shaky at times and the jump-cuts come a bit too often, especially in the beginning when. #VeraFarmiga, #PatrickWilson, #FlorencePugh, #JonathanVanks, #ElizabethMcGovern, and #SamNeill don't get anything to do, but Neeson still keeps the entire thing rolling with help from director #JaumeColletSerra. 评论内容：The Commuter - O Passageiro - Em exibição nos cinemas UCI. Neste intenso thriller de acção, Liam Neeson é Michael, um vendedor de seguros que vê a sua viagem diária para o emprego transformar-se numa série de reviravoltas bem fora da rotina. Depois de ser abordado por um misterioso estranho, Michael é forçado a desvendar a identidade de um passageiro escondido algures no seu comboio antes que este chegue à última paragem. À medida que luta contra o tempo para resolver este puzzle, Michael vai-se apercebendo que um mortífero plano se está a desenrolar e que ele está inadvertidamente preso no centro da conspiração criminosa, que coloca em perigo a sua vida e a segurança dos restantes passageiros. THE COMMUTER – O PASSAGEIRO assinala o regresso da dupla Jaume Collet-Serra, na realização e Liam Neeson num novo grande papel de ação. O elenco conta ainda com Vera Farmiga, Patrick Wilson, Sam Neil, Elizabeth McGovern e Jonathan Banks. 评论内容：🚨🚨 RECOMENDACIÓN CELULOSA 🚨🚨 The Commuter / El Pasajero es un thriller de acción franco-británico-estadounidense dirigido por Jaume Collet-Serra, y escrito por Byron Willinger y Philip de Blasi. Protagonizada por Liam Neeson, Vera Farmiga, Sam Neill, Elizabeth McGovern, Jonathan Bancos, y Patrick Wilson. La película fue estrenada en los Estados Unidos el 12 de enero de 2018, por Lionsgate, y en el Reino Unido el 19 de enero de 2018, por StudioCanal. 评论人：doisjelevoir
评论时间：2018-01-26
评论内容：Petit voyage dans un train de la Banlieue New Yorkaise avec The Passenger. Pour ce Thriller-Action, le réalisateur espagnol Jaume Collet-Serra va retrouver son acteur phare Liam Neeson. Et le moins que l’on puisse dire c’est que cette fois l’alchimie ne fonctionnera pas. On part sur une histoire assez basique. Un homme qui vient de se faire licencier rentre chez lui part un train de banlieue. Une femme s’assoie à côté de lui et lui propose de l’argent en échange d’un petit service. Un choix qui fera basculer la vie de Michael MacCauley. Le casting a beau être intéressant, notamment avec le duo de Conjuring (Vera Farmiga & Patrick Wilson), cela ne compense pas un scénario beaucoup trop prévisible. J’aurai aimé plus de retournement de situation dans une trame qui se devine assez rapidement. De plus, un événement survenant vers la fin vous fera logiquement penser : « Mais en réalité tout ce qui vient de s’écouler été inutile ». Certes, il y a une belle tentative pour compenser ça par un rythme assez soutenu. Et je dois le reconnaitre je ne me suis pas du tout ennuyé durant le film. Mais malheureusement … les scènes d’action sont vraiment improbable. C’est donc avec un sentiment plutôt négatif que je suis sorti de la salle. Ma critique plus détaillée disponible sur ma chaîne YouTube en lien dans ma biographie. #ThePassenger #TheCommuter #LiamNeeson #JaumeColletSerra #Film #Critique #Cinema

评论内容：[ Review phim chiếu rạp - The Commuter/ Hành khách bí ẩn ] . Thực sự là bản thân không mấy xem phim US-UK nên nhớ được tên và yêu thích một diễn viên nào đó thì cũng là rất hiếm 😂 . Cảm nhận về phim The Commuter khá trọn vẹn và ổn. Các tình tiết, các nhân vật và cách xử lý tình huống cũng trôi chảy. Để mà nói thì đoạn đầu khá dễ nhàm chán và hơi buồn ngủ chút do nó phác hoạ lại daily life của diễn viên chính cộng thêm bối cảnh chính trong tàu điện nên có chút tối. Một số cảnh nguy hiểm như đánh nhau hay suýt chết cũng hơi sợ chút 😅 . Vẫn nhớ câu nói "What kind of person are you" - phải chọn lựa giữa tính mạng của những người thân yêu trong gia đình hoặc của những hành khách xa lạ trên chuyến tàu quả không dễ. Nhưng hãy cứ tin rằng công lý luôn chiến thắng. . Lâu mới xem được một bộ phim chiếu rạp mà khá ưng. Cũng có tình tiết điều tra suy luận nên cũng gây tò mò chút. Sau một thời gian xem ma quỷ với trinh thám thì thể loại này lại khiến mình hứng thú.

评论内容：上了大學之後真的很少跑電影院了，以前有事沒事都跟朋友跑哈拉，跟人約出門也大多是跑電影院。 現在很多電影都是改編或續集電影，再不然就是舊片重拍，原創劇本的好電影真的越來越少，會驅使我看完預告片後馬上衝電影院的電影也越來越少了。之前看到【疾速救援】的電影海報，片名跟連恩尼遜讓我直接聯想到【空中救援】跟即刻救援系列（片商們能夠想些有創意一點的片名嗎？），很喜歡推理類型的電影，所以當下就決定要去刷這部。 看完後的感想跟預期差不多，劇情包含著懸疑推理的氛圍，再用些許的動作戲來點綴其中，最後的緊張感跟高潮部分也做得很棒，重點就是連恩尼遜真的太帥了，高大的身影、渾厚的嗓音、銳利的眼神和俐落的身手，最帥的老人非他莫屬(雖然我媽一直堅持是史恩康納萊)。 話說官方釋出了很多風格酷炫的電影海報，但台灣就一定要用最low的那款(因為連恩尼遜的臉最清楚)覺得可惜 #疾速救援 #thecommuter #liamneeson

Die Story selbst ist deutlich spannender als erwartet, hat einige Wendungen, ist super inszeniert und spannend. Man kann die ganze Zeit miträtseln. Erst wen er sucht, dann wer der böse ist. Außer man ist mit meiner Freundin im Kino - die wusste nach etwa 10 Minuten (nach dem im Trailer angeschnittenen Angebot) bescheid. Und sie behielt recht. Wie immer. Allerdings war das auch mein erster Gedanken. Den Film kann man sich auf jeden Fall im Kino ansehen, ich war durchgehend gut unterhalten (obwohl die ersten 20 Minuten nur Charakteraufbau war) und die Inszenierung schreit nach riesiger Leinwand und Popcorn.🍿 Viel spaß ☺️ Und wenn ihr den Film gesehen habt, schreibt mir eure Meinung dazu. 评论人：jimbobtalksmovies
评论时间：2018-01-25
评论内容：The Commuter (2018) Movie Review #thecommuter #moviereview #jimbobtalksmovies. SPOILERS (You have been warned). This is the first movie of 2018 I'm reviewing, The Commuter is a mixture of Non-Stop, Taken and Speed all in one if you ask me, is that a bad thing? No it's not but it is something we've all seen before. The Commuter stars Liam Neeson as Michael, an ex cop, husband and father who commutes on a train every day for work until one day he loses his job. On the train he is confronted by a strange woman who asks him to find a person on the train who does not belong and in return he gets $100,000. This movie is a race against the clock as Neeson puts all his best efforts and skills he learnt as a cop to try and find the mysterious character known as Prin who is aboard the train before his family is killed. The Commuter has great action sequences, it has 2 very good fight scenes that don't rely on great stunt work but make it work. Neeson once again is brilliant as the action hero but there are a few plot holes in this movie and it's nothing we haven't seen before, The Commuter is very much like Non-Stop but on a train. Overall there is great acting in this movie and great action scenes but brings nothing new to the table, The Commuter gets #7.5/10 from @JimbobTalksMovies. #thecommuterjimbobtalksmovies #actionfilmreviewsjimbobtalksmovies.

评论内容：The Commuter: This time he's on a train and it's nearly just as much fun as the "non-stop" plane. Also the Warren's from the conjuring take a break from ghosts and dabble in action but add a nice charm to the character of the film. Liam Neeson is what you come to expect in these style of films but there's nothing wrong with that, it's his niche!! I'm glad they kept the character the same age as Neeson himself, he shows at 60 you can still throw quite a few punches and he always has that commanding presence which adds to the tone of his likeable characters. I personally found the 2nd half better than the first. It felt quite comparable to the film Speed (not as good) towards the end. Especially with the intensity of the music and slightly comparable situation. Overall its alot of fun, you go to see these sort of films for the entertaining action and the thrill of the main characters journey and challenges. I was looking forward to this film as I've always enjoyed films with trains, I don't know why but I always find that setting intense and thrilling and enjoyable to watch. Jaume Collet-Serra - 3/5 - FILM REVIEW - Final Part The direction by Jaume Collet-Serra is grounded as well it can be on a train-location and is appropriately silly when it needs to be when the film shows its flair for action. I did like the opening montage however, that shows the day-to-day life of It's a film that's fully aware of what a Liam Neeson action film is, overdoses a little bit with the concept, gives Neeson plenty of arse to kick and he kicks it bloody well in one one-take fight sequence. So I suppose this film might deserve a 2/5 rating, right? Well it goes back to point I made at the start of this: there's a time and a place for a Liam Neeson action flick. It's self-aware, has an interesting if flawed concept that falls flat eventually and knows what it wants to do as a straight-up action film. The kind of mindless action film that used to get produced and released a lot in the 80's and 90's. It's the kind of film that you might think would be worth it on home-release, but in all honesty, if you don't take the film too seriously, it might just be worth the £5 film ticket - but perhaps not more. It does it's job in being a very flawed entertaining Liam Neeson action vehicle. #thecommuter #thecommuterfilm #jaumecolletserra #2018 #liamneeson #verafarmiga #patrickwilson #jonathanbanks #elizabethmcgovern #samneill #film #filmreview #instamovies #instafilm #action #thriller

评论内容：The Commuter (2018) dir. Jaume Collet-Serra - 3/5 - FILM REVIEW - Part 2 Admittedly, I haven't actually seen Taken in full, nor have I seen any of the action movies that he has starred in recent years; I've just never really had a chance to get into them and watch them properly for some reason. I think it's important to remember that there's a special place reserved in cinemas for the straight-forward, hard and tough-as-nails action/crime/thriller genre movies akin to those of 70s Hollywood films. The sort of films that you could just sit back, watch, take it in and just enjoy. Neeson has managed to do something really special over the last decades with his career in this respect, being involved in the sort of films that you can watch and be entertained by very easily. The beauty of The Commuter is in it's Hitchcock-like simplicity in terms of the plot (at first). This gradually deteriorates however and less favourable when it overdoses on the action part way through. An ex-cop turned normal insurance salesman (those cop "skills" will come in handy no doubt...wink-wink) on a train, put in the right place at the right time, by the wrong people for the wrong reasons, forced to do some bad things. A labyrinthine game of Saw-like proportions begins; it's a race against time, a race against Neeson's own paranoia, where everyone on board the train is his target. It's the simple and one-location game that takes place and the films thriller moments that makes this entertaining. #thecommuter #thecommuterfilm #jaumecolletserra #2018 #liamneeson #verafarmiga #patrickwilson #jonathanbanks #elizabethmcgovern #samneill #film #filmreview #instamovies #instafilm #action #thriller

Maybe he does this in different countries, maybe he does this whilst taking a taxi or plane trip or against wolves in the wild. Pretty well if you're looking if you're not looking for much in consistency and just want to sit back for a silly watch. Since Neeson's career took a major turning point in 2008 with the release of Taken, he redefined his career and has been in the action film business since and shows no signs of stopping any time soon. As well as being a formidable actor with tremendous gravitas (see Schindler's List, Gangs of New York, Batman Begins, Kingdom of Heaven) he lends himself to the action movie genre very well, delivering capable performances whilst delivering on the action-front from a physical perspective, putting effort into the fighting and action sequences. #thecommuter #thecommuterfilm #jaumecolletserra #2018 #liamneeson #verafarmiga #patrickwilson #jonathanbanks #elizabethmcgovern #samneill #film #filmreview #instamovies #instafilm #action #thriller

评论人：moviesta.hj
评论时间：2018-01-25
评论内容：커뮤터 18.01.24. 2.5/5.0 비록 흥행 면에서 두각을 나타내지는 못하더라도 보는 재미만큼은 쏠쏠할 것 같은 영화들이 한번에 쏟아진 금주 개봉작 중 첫 관람작으로 리암 니슨의 <커뮤터>를 택했다. (정확히는 퇴근 시간에 맞는 유일한 영화가 이 영화였다.) 자움 콜렛 세라 감독과 리암 니슨 배우가 네번째로 호흡을 맞춘 이 작품은 감독의 전작들처럼 특별한 건 없더라도 최소한의 재미만큼은 선사한다. 다만 그것이 <논스톱>에서의 그것과 너무나도 유사하다는 것이 문제지만. _ 영화는 10년간 일했던 보험회사에서 해고당한 전직 경찰 마이클이 우연히 엄청난 사건에 휘말리게 되며 겪는 일들을 그려나간다. 어느 때와 마찬가지로 통근 열차를 통해 퇴근하던 마이클은 의문의 여성 조안나에게 이상한 제안을 받게 되고 그 제안을 거절할 새도 없이 그는 가족의 목숨까지 위협받는 신세가 되어버린다. _ 영화에서 마이클이 수행해야 하는 임무는 간단하다. 조안나가 제안한대로, 혹은 명령한대로 기차가 콜드스프링 역에 도착하는 30분 안에 프린이라는 가명의 인물과 그의 가방을 찾아내야한다는 것. 설사 그가 그 임무를 중간에 포기하거나 제3자에게 그에 대해 터놓을 시 즉각적으로 누군가가 위험에 처한다는 사실을, 그리고 그의 가족마저 안전하지 않다는 사실을 알게 된 입장에서 마이클은 프린이라는 인물을 무사히 찾아내기 위해 애써야만 하는 상황에 처한다. _ 앞서 언급한대로 영화는 최소한의 재미는 충분히 자아낸다. 영화를 보다보면 자연스레 조안나라는 여성의 정체가 무엇인지, 그리고 그녀가 찾기를 원하는 프린이라는 인물은 대체 누구인지 파헤치는 마이클에게 이입하게 되고 나 역시도 과연 누가 프린일까를 계속 추리하게 된다. 주인공이 열차 안이라는 밀폐된 공간에서 사건과 밀접한 관련이 있는 누군가를 찾아내야만 한다는 점에서 지난해 말 개봉한 <오리엔트 특급 살인>을 떠올리게 만들기도 한다. _ 다만 영화는 끝끝내 긴장감을 최대치로 끌어내지는 못한다. 의문의 여성 조안나가 영화 내내 마이클이 누군가에게 도움을 처할 때, 혹은 누군가를 의심할 때마다 즉각적으로 그에게 연락을 취하고 더욱 상황을 위태롭게 만드는데 그러한 과정의 대부분이 그저 우연스럽게 느껴진다. 더불어 프린의 정체와 함께 그 인물을 추적하는 또다른 누군가의 정체가 밝혀지는 극후반부 역시 충격적이기보단 어딘가 느슨하고 밋밋하기만 하다. _ 무엇보다 영화의 가장 큰 단점은, 첫 문단에 썼던 바와 같이 감독의 전작이자 마찬가지로 리암 니슨과 호흡을 맞춘 영화 <논스톱>의 전개와 너무나도 유사한다는 것이다. <커뮤터>에서는 전직 경찰로, <논스톱>에서는 항공수사관으로 등장하는 리암 니슨은 두 영화에서 모두 정체 모를 누군가에게 협박을 당하며 그 범인을 찾아냄과 동시에 승객들의 안전을 지키기 위해 노력한다. 그리고 그의 다소 부자연스러운 행동들은 그 자신이 사건의 용의자로 내몰리게 되는 결과까지 낳고 마는 것까지 똑 닮아있다. _ 다시 말해, 그저 공간적 배경이 비행기가 아닌 열차로 바뀌었을 뿐 거의 모든 것이 <논스톱>과 유사하다보니 어느 순간부터는 이토록 안일하고 무성의하게 느껴지는 감독의 연출에 그저 짜증이 나기까지 한다. 우디 앨런 감독이 <매치 포인트>와 너무나도 닮아있는 <이레셔널 맨>을 내놓았을 때처럼 제아무리 뛰어난 감독이라도 그의 영화를 거의 그대로 답습한다면 영 못 미덥게만 느껴지기 마련인 만큼 이 자가복제 역시 어딘가 씁쓸하게만 느껴진다. _ 리암 니슨은 자움 콜렛 세라와 함께 한 네 작품 <언노운>, <논스톱>, <런 올 나이트>, 그리고 이 영화 <커뮤터>부터 그의 대표작 <테이큰>과 <툼스톤> 등에 이르기까지 어딘가 비슷한 성격, 비슷한 직업, 비슷한 환경에 처한 인물을 연이어 연기해왔다. 그리고 이번 영화를 보면서 확실히 느낀 것은, 더이상 이른바 리암 니슨 표 액션영화는 신선하게 다가오기 힘들 것이란 점이다. 죽을 때까지 액션 영화를 하겠다고 선언한 만큼 그의 액션 영화에 대한 미련을 꺾을 수는 없어보이지만 최소한 자움 콜렛 세라 감독과는 더이상 함께 하지 않는 것이 그의 남은 커리어에도 도움되지 않을까 싶다. 이제 부디 그만.. _ #영화스타그램 #cgv #cgv평촌 #커뮤터 #자움콜렛세라 #리암니슨 #베라파미가 #패트릭윌슨 #샘닐 #TheCommuter #JaumeColletSerra #LiamNeeson #VeraFarmiga #PatrickWilson #SamNeill #2018년11번째극장관람작

评论人：fantastic.mr.movies
评论时间：2018-01-24
评论内容：The Commuter- 7/10 •A common businessman is caught in the middle of a conspiracy on the way home• The Commuter impressed me in a lot of ways I didn’t expect it to. For an action movie I found it surprising that most scenes were dialogue driven and the film was very heavy on plot. While it’s always exciting to watch people beat the crap out of each other for two hours straight, I found this gave the film lots of depth, allowing the full investment and attention of the audience, and causing an action scene (when it does occur) to have all the more impact and intensity. Another thing that is always important is that cause is given to the main character and in the Commuter I feel like relationships were very established. If they weren’t you wouldn’t care who died or why, or even about the main character at all. On top of that, the logic for this movie was rock solid. If I was ever questioning the reasoning of the main character, the problem would immediately be explained or resolved. My problem with this movie is unfortunately a big one. While the hand to hand fight scenes were fantastic to watch, often taking you right into them, the de-railing of the train was extremely dragged out and felt absolutely unnecessary. Considering this was supposed to be the climax of the movie it left me dissatisfied and wishing they would’ve taken it a different route. Other than that I really enjoyed The Commuter and thought it was an exciting movie that offers more than you’d expect it to. #movies #thecommuter #commuter #liamneeson #moviereviews #fantasticmrmovies

La quatrième collaboration entre Liam Neeson et Jaume Collet-Sera se déroule cette fois-ci à bord d'un train. C'est un quasi huis clos plutôt efficace même si ça manque de tension. On ne sent pas vraiment de menace et on a du mal à se mettre à la place du personnage. Le scénario est plutôt bon même si ça manque de rebondissements. Par contre, les effets spéciaux sont pour la majorité plutôt loupés et on a l'impression qu'ils ont quelques années de retard. Liam Neeson fait du Liam Neeson des années 2010 et commence, à l'instar de son personnage, à fatiguer un peu. Bref, c'est assurément un très bon film de dimanche soir sur TF1. Est Ce que ça vaut de se déplacer? 评论人：elite_critiques
评论时间：2018-01-23
评论内容：“Lives Are On The Line.” ♦️DIRECTED BY: Jaume Collet-Serra STARRING: Liam Neeson, Vera Farmiga, and Patrick Wilson PLOT SUMMARY: Insurance salesman Michael MacCauley is on his daily commute home, which quickly becomes anything but routine. After being contacted by a mysterious stranger, Michael is forced to uncover the identity of a hidden passenger on the train before the last stop. As he works against the clock to solve the puzzle, he realizes a deadly plan is unfolding, and he is unwittingly caught up in a criminal conspiracy that carries life and death stakes for everyone on the train. PROS: -Liam Neeson (successfully plays “his” role...struggling family man in trouble) Interesting Concept (makes viewers think what they would do in the situation) CONS: -Predictable Plot -Lack of Tension/Intensity -Leaves Unanswered Questions BOTTOM LINE: The Commuter is next movie of the director/actor team-up between Jaume Collet-Serra and Liam Neeson. These two are respon for sible similar action movies in the past together such as, Unknown, Non-Stop, and Run All Night. I went into this movie hoping to receive a film similar to Non-Stop, due to myself personally enjoying that film a lot, but instead, I got a dulled down version with this movie. Since seeing previous films from this director, I knew exactly where the story was going to go. I turned to my friend, who I saw this with, and told him who was behind the whole hostage plot within the first five minutes of the movie. I can’t really recommend this movie because I found myself falling asleep during parts of the movie, that were intended to be intense. RATING: C+/5.5/2.5⭐️ Comment below on whether you agree or disagree and make sure to like this picture! ♦️ #thecommuter #studiocanal #EliteCritiques

Liam Neeson stars as Michael MacCauley a businessman who is caught up in a criminal conspiracy during his daily commute home. If you think this is just another Liam Neeson movie with Liam Neeson being Liam Neeson and doing Liam Neeson type things...you would be correct! Let’s be honest at this point your not going to see a movie starring Liam Neeson and expect an intricate storyline or world class cinematography. But what you can always expect is a fun ride. The Commuter delivers on that promise with just that, plenty of action and a few good twist every now and then. Pros: Hitchcock: What makes this film fun is that it really seems to draw on an Alfred Hitchcock vibe of whodunnit? Vera Farmiga: best known for her roles as Norma Bates in Bates Motel & The Departed. Farmiga always delivers a convincingly good role. In this case, as a great antagonist Cons: I mean to really pick at this film -Expected corny Lines -While some of the twist were good. A few were so typical you could see a mile away Overall Rating 7/10 #movies #liamneeson #thecommuter #film #cinemark

评论内容：The Commuter. Seen this twice now, both in IMAX! Films like these rarely get made anymore, but when they do they sure do pack a lot of suspense, thrills and old school action that really make for a captivating fun ride! Directed by Juame Collet-Serra and starring Liam Neeson The Commuter marks their fourth collaboration together (Uknown, Non-Stop, Run All Night and now this) and the two deliver yet another thrilling, edge of your seat action film that does well in mixing mystery and action into one! Serra is one of the best directors in the industry, and does not get the credit he deserves! Neeson, once again, kicks serous ass and proves why he is one of the best action hero's of our time! This film was entertaining and had only a small budget of 30 million dollars, which is quite low compared to a majority of action films made these days! Serra and Neeson should definitely reteam for a fifth film together! 评论内容：My Rating: 55/100 The Commuter is the newest action film in the line-up of action movies starring Liam Neeson. This movie had some really cool actions sequences that were very well directed, but the overall film lacked in emotional depth and character development. The Commuter is just a fun action movie that is not really meant to blow audiences away. I didn’t really like this movie, and that’s because of the extremely predictable plot twists and very cringe-worthy performances. The Commuter is fun, but that’s it. The two main redeeming qualities to this movie are the action-set pieces and the storyline. Neste intenso thriller de acção, Liam Neeson é Michael, um vendedor de seguros que vê a sua viagem diária para o emprego transformar-se numa série de reviravoltas bem fora da rotina. Depois de ser abordado por um misterioso estranho, Michael é forçado a desvendar a identidade de um passageiro escondido algures no seu comboio antes que este chegue à última paragem. À medida que luta contra o tempo para resolver este puzzle, Michael vai-se apercebendo que um mortífero plano se está a desenrolar e que ele está inadvertidamente preso no centro da conspiração criminosa, que coloca em perigo a sua vida e a segurança dos restantes passageiros. Still dissapointed that Paddington 2 didn't make it, but at least it jumped The Commuter to become 6th. 评论人：imoviesreview
评论时间：2018-01-22
评论内容：The Commuter Time to kick my 2018 movies off with a Liam Neeson action movie. I’ll be honest with you, this movie doesn’t look good. It looks like another cheesy action flick, but Liam Neeson is the reason I’m seeing this movie. The guy has had his fair share of bad movies, but this is from the same guy who did Non-Stop. Non-Stop looked like a cheesy action movie, but it actually turned out to be good, I enjoyed most of it. I’m willing to give this movie a chance. I do find some cheesy action movies more enjoyable then the average movie goer cause I like action. Action movies are an easy to do but hard to pull off form of entertainment. I’m not expecting much from this movie, I’m just expecting to be entertained. So with that in mind let’s see what we have in store for us. A businessman is caught up in a criminal conspiracy during his daily commute home. I definitely got what the director was trying to do here, I just think he tried to do too much. This movie starts off simple enough, then once the main plot starts things get really out of hand. I was asking more questions then this movie was answering. Pretty much this movie sets up a bunch of rules for the main character to follow, if he doesn’t follow these rules his family dies, but the main character breaks a bunch of these rules in the second act and nothing happens. There were so many plot holes with this movie that I lost enjoyment by the third act. Also the more this movie goes on, the more insane this movie gets. I was able to find some enjoyment in the middle when the mystery aspect was still in play. So I can give this movie some credit for the second act, but that’s not much considering how confusing this movie can be. The Commuter tries to recapture the mystery aspect of Non-Stop, but the more information this movie adds to the plot the more confusing it is. Much like any other Liam Neeson action movie, he carries the whole movie. He plays Michael MacCauley who’s an ex cop who is taking the train home one day and he must find a suspect a woman is looking for or else people die. It’s easy to have sympathy for this character and he is likable and noble. Continued in Comments.

评论人：fairfilmreviews
评论时间：2018-01-22
评论内容：THE COMMUTER – 2018 STARS: 6/10 While I think it is fair to say that this is a film in which the action sequences and CGI actually serve the storyline rather than rule it, too much prevenance is still given to eye-candy visuals, resulting in an undeniably entertaining but both implausible and overdone ride on something as basic as a commuter train. The piece is exceptionally well edited and filmed though – or perhaps creatively is the more appropriate word, for the visuals are neither sweeping nor seamless, merely intriguing. Indeed the entire piece reeks of that same intrigue; that fascinating yet decidedly staged vibe that grabs you and draws you in, despite everything your heart and mind tells you. Yes, perhaps you can never be fully engrossed in a story that is so obviously fabricated, but you can certainly be entertained – and that is this film's main plus as far as I am concerned; the ability to hold an audience on an unemotionally connected level. Not unlike one of those cheap but addictive cops and robbers style shows one might see in the evening on television, "The Commuter" somehow manages – with, literally, a hundred suspects, a hundred questions and a virtual time bomb ticking away throughout – to be drawn out, predictable and ultimately unimpressive . . . yet still watchable; still something you would sit down to and not move on from. There is some part of all of us – perhaps – that relishes hours upon hours of unabashed improbability and even as you pretend disinterest in this piece I warrant you will find yourself coming back to that one fateful catch question: what would you do?

评论人：planned_imperfect
评论时间：2018-01-22
评论内容：Written by Carlos Crestwell Movie #3 The Commuter. At this point what can you say. Liam Neeson has never been short on work but sense Taken released in 2008 he has been in a steady stream of these well written suspense protagonist vs X dangerous antagonist. He does them very well and as much as you’d like to say enough. Neeson is always so compelling to to sit down and watch that you can’t help but check out his films. This role is no different as he pairs up again with director Jaume Collet-Serra who he’s been around the block with a few times (Non-Stop, Run All Night, Unknown). In this role he plays former NYPD detective turned insurance salesmen Michael MacCauley. A family man with a repetitively boring existence working a 9-5 to support his family. He gets put into a dangerous situation by a mysterious stranger on his usual train route home and Liam Neeson starts to do his thing. Co-stars Vera Farmiga and Patrick Wilson help make up the small bit of star power in this film but it’s well executed seeing how most these films never lose sight of Neeson as their focus. Still another well executed suspense film with very few complaints. These films rarely get too deep in the weeds which is probably a good thing. #Thecommuter #Copperwiire #Loscinema2018

评论内容：The Commuter For god sake Liam, keep your family with you at all times! Now the story of this film is a little bazaar, but it keeps you gripped even if it is set on one of the worst forms of public transport. The film follows Michael MacCauley (Liam Neeson) on his daily commute to his job as an insurance salesman. He has had this job for 10 years and sadly gets let go. On his train ride home that day, a women named Joanna joins Michael in the seat opposite. She posses a hypothetical question where he has to do one thing and in return can earn $100,000. This hypothetical turns out to be real when Michael must find a passenger on the train who doesn't belong who goes by the allias of "Prynne" before Cold springs station or there will be consequences. He just has to find "Prynne" to get the $100,000, but as time runs out and his family become endangered, Michael must figure out who he can and can't trust. Check the Trailer here Now being a big Liam Neeson fan i enjoyed this film. To me all his films are the same, the plot is changed up a bit but most of the films feel formulaic and i found myself thinking alot about Taken. This film although different has alot of action and Neesons character has the lives his family at stake again. For God sake Liam, keep your family with you at all time! That being sad although the movie feels similar to his others, it is still enjoyable and keeps you engaged as you try to work out who "Prynne" is . No spoilers but I totally knew who "Prynne" was. The movie is decent enough, plus Liam Neeson running through the train causing havoc, who doesn't wanna see that. My Film Rating 5/10 🎥🍿 #film #filmreview #filmgradreview #movie #cinema #thecommuter #liamneeson #action #thriller #review #train

评论人：jackoransom97
评论时间：2018-01-22
评论内容：An entertaining (and in some places very good) thriller movie. Basic overview without spoiling, is that on his commute back from work Liam Neeson's character is approached by a mysterious woman (Vera Farmiga) who offers him $100,000 to find someone on the train who doesn't belong there and it escalates from there. All the cast are great Neeson is as good as the character type as usual, Patrick Wilson & Vera Farmiga are good supports. Also one thing I didn't expect was too actually find the train passengers as interesting, likeable and well written as they were. The film has some excellent writing and tense directing most so in the dialogue and scenes where he's starting awkward conversations to try and work out who's who and when he's is pacing up and down train trying to work out the situation. The film excels in these areas as they are more thrilling than the action sequences, one of which is awesome (Neeson fighting a dude with a guitar) and delivering an epic one liner after, however the other main fight sequences are just average and you've seen them loads of times before. Speaking of seen before this film doesn't bring much new to the table, if you've seen 'Non-Stop' or other Neeson movies you've basically watched this (not that's that's a bad thing). The ending is fairly predictable and the third act slows down a bit and makes the pacing a bit off and there's some dodgy CGI in places. Overall this a entertaining movie that does what it sets out to do and it's worth a watch for sure 👍🏻#thecommuter#2018#liamneeson#verafarmiga#patrickwilson#jaumecolletserra#movie#film#cinema

评论人：moviemaniac.id
评论时间：2018-01-22
评论内容：The Commuter (2018) Movie Maniac rating: 3.5/5 It's the fourth collaboration between Liam Neeson and director Jaume Collet-Serra, and it's also the 7th time Liam Neeson played a tough guy character ever since he starred in Taken. The Commuter feels like a combination of 2011's Source Code (for the train setting) and 2014's Non-Stop (for the mystery killer on board of a moving transportation, and Liam Neeson presence). But despite the average reviews by fellow critics, I really enjoy this movie and this movie is better than Unknown, Non-Stop, and Run All Night. I personally like the editing of the beginning of the movie, the fast forward scenes are unique. The story, well there is no such thing in real world, is unbelievable but it works right on this movie, the villain resembles the villain in 2008's Eagle Eye in which the villain has an eye and ear anywhere and can do anything that sounds impossible. Liam Neeson plays the character very well, mostly like his previous good family man and highly skilled tough guy character. The action scenes are good, some of it are thrilling in fact. The movie really entertains and keeps you guessing until the climax of the movie. Another thing to add, I personally like the drama side of this movie where Liam Nesson's character got laid off from work and he has a burden to finance his kid's tuition. It is realistic and depicts the harsh thing in our lives. In my opinion, if you like Liam Neeson and his previous action movies, then you must see this movie. Don't expect a realistic storyline, just enjoy the movie and have a good time. #thecommuter #liamneeson #movies #film #hollywood #review #hobby #action #2018 @thecommuterfilm @lionsgate @cinema.21 @cinemaxxtheater @cgv.id @cinemagsnews

评论人：indomoviereview
评论时间：2018-01-21
评论内容：The Commuter is a 2018 action thriller film directed by Jaume Collet-Serra. The film follows a man who is unwittingly recruited into a murder conspiracy after meeting a mysterious woman while on his daily train commute. Pros: I go in with zero knowledge of what this film is about and a very low expectation (since you know, it’s a January movie). To my surprise, this is a very solid and entertaining movie with a rather unique premise. It leans heavily towards the mystery-thriller aspect, which is a truly refreshing idea to make the movie stand out (at least for the first half of the runtime). It raises some interesting questions about the morality of the main character, and in a way also allows the character develop in a more entertaining fashion. Liam Neeson’s performance is fantastic and he has a very impressive fight scene around the second act of the film. Cons: I’d like to call the main issue with this film “the escalation problem”. The film does some very questionable and inconsistent decisions throughout the story just in order to escalate the stakes higher and higher every time. At some point it turns from an engaging crime thriller with detective works into an over-the-top full blown action film for no apparent reason other than trying to make the film seemingly have a bigger stakes. There are a lot of plotholes made during this process and honestly I’d rate this with a much higher score had it simply been a contained thriller inside a train. Verdict: The Commuter is a very pleasant surprise for January movies. It’s an engaging thriller film with interesting premise, although at some point the film tries to bite more than it can chew. Rating: 3.5/5 #movie #movies #film #review #cinema #moviebuff #moviereview #moviereviews #moviefan #movielover #moviestagram #moviecritic #filmbuff #filmreview #reviewfilm #instafilm #instamovie #instamovies #cinephile #cinephilecommunity #greatmovie #action #hollywood #thecommuterimr #thecommuter #liamneeson #thriller #crimethriller #mystery

评论时间：2018-01-21
评论内容：The Commuter (2018) - film review The Commuter presents a compelling mystery that keeps me invested. The plot is interesting and the mystery unveils smoothly. The main character Michael played by Liam Neeson is a character that has a believable motivation for his actions in the film, which also helps his character to be one that is easy to root for. The action scenes are not bad, but nothing new or especially well done is presented. The opening sequence of the film is quite well made with interesting editing style. The CGI is poorly done but fortunately it isn’t relied too much by the film. Some scenes challenge the edge of possibility and this can be slightly annoying. Overall the film is not particularly inventive or brilliantly crafted, but it is undoubtedly a decent and somewhat enjoyable watch. 7/10 #thecommuter #film #movie #filmreview

评论人：movies_of_the_future
评论时间：2018-01-21
评论内容：MOVIE REVIEW: The Commuter [2018] Director: Jaume Collet-Serra Stars: Liam Neeson, Vera Farmiga, Patrick Wilson, Jonathan Banks, Ella-Rae Smith Colin McFarlane, Shazad Latif and Sam Neill Review: Who would’ve thought star Liam Neeson and director Jaume Collet-Serra would’ve done four collaborations together now. While Unknown, Non-Stop and Run All Night aren’t anything amazing, they’re still solid action movies, as is The Commuter. While the film is in many ways Non-Stop on a train, it’s still a fun, engaging thriller. Liam Neeson as always puts in 110%, even though he’s definitely getting “too old for this sh*t”. He’s so uncompromisingly likeable and just someone so easy to get behind. Vera Farmiga was disappointingly bland, but her part didn’t require much. Patrick Wilson delivered strong in a bigger role than I had expected. Sam Neill was also a surprise as I wasn’t expecting to see, but a pleasant one at that. All the other cast members on the train were also fantastic. Director Jaume Collet-Serra doesn’t make movies you think about for days after days, but he excels at just engaging you for 2 hours and making you walk out pleased. Collet-Serra also masters at contained thrillers, brilliantly using every location and making the most of them. The plot is also genuinely intriguing. Of course it’s filled with many cliche and predictable elements, but all in all it kept me invested. I don’t think The Commuter has as great rewatch value as let’s say Non-Stop or Run All Night, but that’s not a negative. Overall, as this’s my first 2018, I think the year is off to a pretty solid start, especially for January. Rating: B- Reviewer: @declanwilson_

评论人：truyenngontinh
评论时间：2018-01-21
评论内容：#ChuyênMụcGiớiThiệuPhimHayDoBạnHoàiĐềCử Tên phim: #HànhKháchBíẨn hay #TheCommuter 🎬 . Nếu vào một ngày nọ, một người lạ mặt đến gặp bạn để nhờ làm 1 việc nho nhỏ, không hại đến bản thân hay người khác nhưng lại có món tiền hậu hĩnh để tạ ơn, bạn sẽ làm chứ? Nhất là khi họ sẽ ứng trước 500 triệu - 1/4 số tiền mà bạn sẽ nhận được nếu hoàn thành công việc? Nhất là khi bạn đang rất cần tiền và vừa bị đuổi việc? . Nhân vật chính trong phim Hành khách bí ẩn đã gặp những điều đó. Ở tuổi 60, là cựu cảnh sát nhưng ông đã dành hơn 10 năm để bán bảo hiểm, để rồi chỉ còn 5 năm nữa đến tuổi về hưu, ông lại bị đuổi việc. Trên chuyến tàu tốc hành về nhà - phương tiện mà ông vẫn sử dụng mỗi ngày trong 10 năm qua để đi đến công ty và trở về, ông đã gặp được một người phụ nữ lạ mặt cùng lời đề nghị như đã nói ở lúc đầu. Mọi chuyện tưởng dễ dàng, ấy thế mà, nhân vật của Liam Neeson lại dính vào vụ rắc rối đầy kinh hoàng. . Nhiệm vụ của ông là phải tìm ra 1 hành khách trên chuyến tàu này với 1 chiếc túi chưa rõ hình dáng. Nếu ông hoàn thành, ông sẽ có 2 tỷ trong tay. Gợi ý duy nhất chính là, đây là người "không ngồi đúng vị trí của mình", nghĩa là đây là lần đầu tiên người đó ngồi trên chuyến tàu tốc hành. Với kinh nghiệm 10 năm đi tàu, ông nhớ rõ mặt của những người khách quen. Việc tìm kiếm 1 người lạ mặt, với ông sẽ không khó. Tuy nhiên, chuyến tàu hôm nay lại có khá nhiều người lạ mặt, và ông phải lọc tất cả. . Tuy vậy, tiền không đơn giản đánh đổi bằng thời gian. Ông phát hiện ra vợ con mình đang là con tin của tổ chức - những người xúi giục ông tìm kiếm người khách và chiếc túi kia. Vô tình mở lời với 1 người khách quen để nhờ báo cảnh sát, ông đã đẩy người bạn của mình vào chỗ chết. Từng người một trên tàu đã lần lượt bị giết chết nếu có biểu hiện tiếp xúc gần với ông. Áp lực về thời gian khi ga cuối cùng cũng là thời điểm kết thúc trò chơi, nỗi lo lắng cho tính mạng vợ con, và trên hết, ông biết rõ mình đang dính vào những kẻ không nên đụng đến. . Nguồn: Hóng Hớt Showbiz Ps: Phim thuộc thể loại bí ẩn, tâm lý, tội phạm. Ai không coi được thể loại này đừng đi coi nhé ^^

评论内容：🎬 REVIEW: The Commuter (2018) ••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••••• Leeham Kneeson is always pleasant to watch. His Irish accent is always pleasant to listen to. 评论人：filmfactsreviews
评论时间：2018-01-21
评论内容：“The Commuter” (2018) stars Liam Neeson and Patrick Wilson with a strong supporting cast. It was directed by Jaume Collet-Serra marking the third time he has worked with Liam Neeson in the lead role. In simple terms, this is exactly what you would expect from a Liam Neeson action movie. Some things were done better, for example I found one of Liam’s best fight scenes to be in this movie using that seemingly one-shot style from Kingsman. Other stuff not so much like the cliche and overboard-ness if the final act. The characters of the movie were all serve-their-role sort of characters, not many dimensions beyond their niche of a role, save for Liam Neeson, who’s character had great setup with motives and personal drive within the third act making him a compelling and relatable character to back. The plot was good. Claustrophobic setting on the train was directed very well with some talented shots throughout the film. But the basic plot premise, to restate was like your typical Liam Neeson action movie. The spectacle was all solid or good till the third act where an abundance of CGI was used and honestly just looked cheap. Add cheap cgi to a predictable and cliche finale it detracts from the movie. All said and done, this was a fun movie. No it wasn’t groundbreaking, and yes it was a run of the mill Liam Neeson Action Movie, but it was a fun time and had a very promising start with the buildup in the first act, great followthrough in the second act getting into the meat of the movie... then no pun intended it kinda de-railed in the third act giving an ending and “twist” that was pretty expected. Overall, a good time. B #TheCommuter #LiamNeeson #Nonstop #2018 #MovieReviews #Actionmovie #train #commuter

评论内容：™ Liam Neeson, aktor gaek yg sudah berusia 65 tahun, kembali membintangi sebuah film aksi, bila dalam Non-Stop dia beraksi didalam sebuah pesawat terbang, kini dia beraksi didalam sebuah Commuter Film ini merupakan kali keempat Neeson bekerja sama dengan sutradara asal Spanyol Jaume Collet-Serra, setelah Unknown, Run All Night dan Non-Stop The Commuter bercerita tentang seorang mantan polisi bernama Michael, selama 10 tahun terakhir dia bekerja sebagai agen asuransi, dan pengguna setia Commuter Ketika keadaan finansialnya sedang tidak bagus, dia dipecat dari tempatnya bekerja, dan dalam perjalanan pulang, seorang wanita misterius menawarkan uang sebesar $100 ribu untuk menemukan seseorang didalam Commuter tersebut Tidak ada hal baru yg ditawarkan Jaume Collet-Serra dalam film ini, jalan cerita yg mudah ditebak, kemudian sedikit main aman dengan karakter yg diperankan oleh Liam Neeson, merupakan dua hal yg membuat film ini menjadi kurang menarik Namun bagi pecinta Liam Neeson, The Commuter tentunya sayang untuk dilewatkan Movie Pages Score 3 ➡ Film ini sedang tayang dibioskop, Jika tidak ada pilihan film lain yg lebih keren, silahkan menonton film ini ⚪ ⚫ ⚪ Ikutin terus Movie Pages untuk mendapatkan Berita, poster dan trailer film film terbaru Jangan lupa Like dan tag teman kamu untuk lihat postingan ini #MovieReview #ReviewFilm #BeritaFilm #PosterFilm #JaumeColletSerra #TheCommuter #LiamNeeson #VeraFarmiga #PatrickWilson #MovieNews #Movie_Pages

评论人：jpcbarron
评论时间：2018-01-21
评论内容：THE COMMUTER; aka “Non-Stop” on a train. The movie stars type-casted Liam Neeson playing an old retired badass who has a loving family, but then an incident onboard insert vehicle, drives him to take matters into his own hands at the same time being set up by the bad guys. It’s basically the same story as Non-Stop (also starring Liam Neeson, and also directed by the same person; Jaume Collet-Serra) but this time, it’s on a train. It is a decent action movie to say the least, it has more of a thriller vibe than an action film, with some twists and turns here and there… you know how it is with this kind of genre. It’s more of a mystery film cause it’s more of finding a specific target with people being obstacles to you. The action scenes I really like too because of how self-contained it is, really giving the film more weight as they made us really feel the claustrophobia cause it just takes place in one train. I will admit, the opening sequence for this movie is one of my favourite parts of the film. I just like the montage and the film’s Score that accompanies it. Will have to say, @roquebanos’ music for the film I really like a lot. It has this really nice relaxing piano piece in the start, mixed with the orchestra, the music may sound minimalistic, but I think it works for an ordinary type of protagonist we follow. It’s an interesting movie to see in theatres, and I personally don’t think it was a waste of money. I think you guys might enjoy it, but just go into it with low expectations cause I did and in the end, I genuinely enjoyed it. In the end, it’s a familiar story that you’ve seen before in a Liam Neeson action movie, it’s just a very self-contained minimalistic action thriller film, that’s enjoyable. So I wanna pass on the question to you. Have you seen The Commuter and what did you think of it? I’d love to know your thoughts in the comments below.
