评论内容：The Commuter - O Passageiro - Em exibição nos cinemas UCI. Neste intenso thriller de acção, Liam Neeson é Michael, um vendedor de seguros que vê a sua viagem diária para o emprego transformar-se numa série de reviravoltas bem fora da rotina. Depois de ser abordado por um misterioso estranho, Michael é forçado a desvendar a identidade de um passageiro escondido algures no seu comboio antes que este chegue à última paragem. À medida que luta contra o tempo para resolver este puzzle, Michael vai-se apercebendo que um mortífero plano se está a desenrolar e que ele está inadvertidamente preso no centro da conspiração criminosa, que coloca em perigo a sua vida e a segurança dos restantes passageiros. THE COMMUTER – O PASSAGEIRO assinala o regresso da dupla Jaume Collet-Serra, na realização e Liam Neeson num novo grande papel de ação. O elenco conta ainda com Vera Farmiga, Patrick Wilson, Sam Neil, Elizabeth McGovern e Jonathan Banks. Título original: The Commuter Data: 2018; Origem: Reino Unido, Estados Unidos da América; Género: Ação, Thriller; 104 Min. 评论内容：《疾速救援》 原本要去爬山，結果下雨，只好改約看電影 沒有任何研究，詮勝同學說哪部就看哪部 一樣沒有任何功課，連預告片都沒看，甚至連海報都不知道長怎樣，我就進電影院 劇情圍繞在一輛火車上 看英文片名可以略知一二 The commuter 通勤者的意思 前段之一講家庭，帶出缺錢的壓力 前段之二講通勤，帶出主場的背景 前段之三講資遣，帶出缺錢的無助 前段之四酒吧談話，帶出主角前身 鋪陳中規中矩，中段從一個神秘女子開始 用一些莫名其妙沒什麼邏輯的話來引導 不只主角一頭霧水，我也一頭霧水 大意是，我給你錢，你幫我找人 原本的假設性問題，突然強迫中獎了 中段有點冗長，大致上就是傲嬌的說不想做，但身體倒是挺誠實的 解謎過程，一點也不精彩，就是我覺得是你，就是你，然後猜錯了 然後不是他的話，那一定是你，啊，又猜錯了 然後一直猜到最後，沒得選了，只有他了，這樣 然後進入後段，為什麼要找他，為什麼要聽話，這樣到底有什麼意義 不雷人的，也沒什麼好雷的 最後的結果，雖然有點那麼一回事也是對啦的感覺 但根本就是白忙 幕後黑手那麼強直接意外殺光光就好了啊 小動作一堆 整體來說，角色情感薄弱 家裡老婆就不懂生活壓力 小孩長大也那模樣 當然可以理解爸媽想給小孩最好的 可是實在沒什麼必要性 小孩想唸州立大學，偏偏要送去唸私立 有錢也就算了，被資遣就打算走歪路也是讓人笑笑 再説，一個辭職警察可以把空調弄壞，讓火車脫離，也是有點多功能 最後朋友上車，翻臉打架 但歸根來說，朋友也是為他好 知道他缺錢，所以私下舉薦他來做 出發點不能說多壞，就是方法不對 結尾也沒有什麼大快人心的劇情 就是唷，差不多就這樣了 覺得可惜的地方蠻多 比如說 家庭親密度不夠 朋友羈絆不深 解題過程鬆散 主角立場不一 幕後動機不明 照我說，如果背後勢力那麼大，外流證據又那麼重要，不如一開始就設計讓火車出軌，一勞永逸 所以說嘛，整體來說，最強老爸還是即刻救援的第一集好看 如果是復仇類的話，還是為了一隻狗滅人整團的「捍衛任務」好看 #電影觀後感 #最強老爸 #thecommuter

评论内容：Sutradara: Jaume Colle Penulis: Byron Willi, Philip de B Bintang Film: Vera Farmiga, Liam Neeson, Patrick Wilson Genre: Action, Crime, Drama Tanggal Rilis: 2018-01-12 Plot Film The Commuter ini merupakan sebuah film terbaru 2018 asal Hollywood. Film ini memiliki genre baru Drama, Mystery, dan Thrilller, untuk sutradaranya akan disutradarai oleh Jauma Colet-Serra, untuk penulis naskah skenario dikuasai oleh Byron Willinger (Screenplay), dan Philip de Blasi. Film ini akan dibintangi para aktor-aktor terkenal di papan atas Hollywood yang akan berperan yaitu Vera Farmiga, Liam Neeson (aktor Utama), Patrick Wilson, Sam Neill, Elizabeth Mc Govern. diawal perilisan perdana film ini menggunakan bahasa Inggris bahasa utama dibioskop kesayangan anda. Sementara film ini akan digarap oleh rumah produksi Ombra Film, Studio Canal. dan The Picture Company. dan dinaungi distributor Lionsgate, VVS Films. Film ini masih menelusuri panjang durasi. Untuk The Picture Company akan merencanakan perilisan perdana pada tanggal 12 Januari (2018) (USA). . Sinopsis Film Film The Commuter ini akan menceritakan tentang seorang pria bernama Liam Veeson, dia adalah seorang pebisnis terkenal yang selalu disibukkan dengan aktivitas yang dihampiri setiap hari. Dari sinilah ketegangan dalam film ini akan dimulai Liam Neeson berada pada situasi yang sangat menegangkan, jika ia tidak melakukan apapun kereta akan mengalami kecelakaan dan nyawa ribuan orang pun terancam. Ia pun harus menggagalkan sesuatu untuk menggagalkan aksinya. Kemudian hari, sebuah peristiwa terjadi didalam Commuter dan pria menjadi aksi saksi terjadinya konpirasi kriminal ketika pulang dari kantornya tersebut. Mengetahui sebuah rencana tan pa sengaja dari sekelompok orang berniat untuk menghancurkan kereta. Disisi lain Neeson harus melakukan guna menghentikan kejahatan tersebut, karena jika sempaikereta ceoat mengalami kecelakaan peritiwwa orang ingin menghancurkan kereta cepat tersebut. Bagi yang penasaran dengan kisah kelanjutan kisahnya, The Commuter akan dirilis perdana menjelang tahun 2018, masih cukup lama Sutradara Jaume Collet-Serra ini akan dirilis pada tanggal 12 Januari (2018) (USA). . #neracafilm #thecommuter

评论内容：NEW EPISODE! (Listen / download) That Film Stew Ep 103 - The Commuter Review (LINK IN BIO) The action thriller The Commuter is directed by Jaume Collet-Serra, and stars Liam Neeson, Vera Farmiga, Patrick Wilson, Jonathan Banks, Elizabeth McGovern, and Sam Neil. Thanks to Anarchy PR (@anarchy_pr), we were given to opportunity to attend an advanced screening of the film. Michael McCauley (played by Liam Neeson), is an ex-cop, now insurance salesman, who is on his daily commute home – taking the metro train. A mysterious stranger (played by Vera Farmiga), offers him $100,000 if he identifies a hidden passenger on his train before the last stop. As he works against the clock to solve the puzzle, he realises he is caught in midst of a deadly criminal conspiracy and that his life and the lives of his fellow passengers are at risk. Does The Commuter manage to stay on track or does the movie get derailed before the credits roll? Check out what we thought in our review (we manage to keep it relatively spoiler-free until about the 10 minute mark). The Commuter opens officially in Australia on Thursday 18th January 2018. 评论内容：最近的共時性，老師推介了量子學老師Marcus 的新書【人生急轉彎】；同學聚會時探討過職場生涯轉營規劃；然後沒頭沒腦地被帶去看了這齣戲。。。竟然也是同一個題目。 想起【陰謀背後】的slogan『到底人生係充滿選擇，定係已經被精心策劃...』悲哀的後者是現實。金融體系，銀行地產，政權醫療。。。無一不操控住每一個人走入去個移動迷宮，迫使人在只談現實和隨心而行中困獸之鬥。 話說回來劇情是牽強的，但主角的處境卻是真實的，要在利益和道德中作出取捨，不是每一個人都可以一直堅定，看著本來是正義凜然的主角為著供樓養妻活兒，人生一步步地退到差點失去自尊和道德，沉重又共嗚，除了「人人為我，我為人人」的BBQ 結局是有點難為情外，其實個半小時都算緊張刺激。曾經是警員也喜歡當警員的主角十年如一地在保險業上班下班，不致於行屍走肉，但人生嘛，就是這樣。。。一天突然就被辭退，生活一下就崩壞，主角就是一刻鐘就走進了『四大風景』（無錢、無工、無屋、無左關係），絕望中被策劃登上亡命列車，懸疑和逃亡外加犧牲小我的人性光輝，瘕疪是即使沒看懂過動作片的我也覺得戲內的打鬥場面有點勉為其難，畢戲裡戲外的主角都已65,70歲了，但年齡重要嗎？戲裡戲外的Liam Neeson都有著一團火應該比較重要。看完輕微地和主角一樣得到第二次的人生，我喜歡一切的小意外，共時性💖 #3⭐️ #逃出迷宮、逃出列車 #thecommuter#LiamNeeson#enjoy#treat#leisure#Synchronicity#petme#comment#rebirth#hkig

评论内容：The Commuter (2018) Director: Jaume Collet-Serra Starring: Liam Neeson, Vera Farmiga, Patrick Wilson, Sam Neill, Elizabeth McGovern 5.5 out of 10. It took three writers to come up with this movie's cliche-riddled script that borrows ideas from Murder on the Orient Express, Flightplan, Red Eye, countless Hitchcock films and even Neeson's previous starrer, Non Stop. Premise is unoriginal while the plot is hackneyed with very predictable bad guys. If you are a Neeson fan, this run-of-the-mill action-thriller will provide you a minor diversion, otherwise, wait for it on DVD or digital. #thecommuter #liamneeson #actionmovie #trainridetohell #train #whodunit

评论人：turpsfilmreview
评论时间：2018-01-20
评论内容："Someone on this train does not belong." #TurpsFilmReview (6/10) THE COMMUTER is yet another collaboration between director Jaume Collet-Sera and Liam Neeson and is in the same vein as previous ventures, 'Unknown' and especially 'Non-Stop'. All three of these films revolve around a mystery that obviously isn't getting solved until the end. My biggest issue with this director (and his scripts) is that he never gives you enough context to solve these mystery films on your own, but then wants to pretend to be intelligent when you can't figure out "whodunit". There's virtually no shock value when you find out the culprit has been hiding off-screen for 99% of the movie. Non-Stop isn't quite as guilty as this film is, but it's just as manipulative in its approach. Collet-Sera just hides pertinent information to be revealed at the end in a really unsatisfactory way. The rest of the plot isn't special either and is entirely predictable. All the twists and turns can be seen from a mile away and character motives are pretty obvious right out of the gate. The reveal of why he was chosen by Vera Farmiga's character for this "experiment", or whatever you wanna call it, is completely ridiculous too. Liam Neeson almost single handedly saves this film from being 105 minutes of dullness with his performance. Say what you will, but Neeson is a master at holding your attention and could make eating a bowl cereal a thrill ride. The rest of the cast including Patrick Wilson, Sam Neill, Jonathan Banks, and Vera Farmiga are all serviceable and provide interesting enough characters. Overall however, THE COMMUTER took a decent idea and made a decent movie out of it. If you're a Neeson fan, there's enjoyment to be had here, but it's no 'Taken'. Thanks for reading.

评论人：pegawai_xl
评论时间：2018-01-20
评论内容：It's been almost a decade since Liam Neeson played as Bryan Mills in Taken and that movie not only became a cult in class B action movie but also created a new sub-genre in action which is Neeson-genre. What is Neeson-genre? These are the movies starring Liam Neeson (of course lah!) as a messed-up/retired cop/ex-cop/agent that find redemption and escalate from zero to hero for the greater good in the movie. How can a generic plot like this become a genre with 9 movies since taken (taken trilogy, the grey, unknown, non-stop, a walk among the tombstones, run all night)? That is because he played as close as underdog he can be. There is no hi-tech weapon nor cool cars backing up. An old guy with sad puppy eyes, deep charismatic voice, a gun, a cellphone and a very particular self-skills to break some bones in a close combat and kick bad guys ass. That is my friends the deadly combination in Neeson-genre. The audience was entertained and the total box-office gross more than half a billion US dollars, not bad. (The production cost are very low for these movies) Back to the movies, as usual no spoiler spills but what I can tell you, according my eyes, this movie is a spiritual sequel of Non-stop. If in Non-stop we got Julliane Moore, in this movie we got The Warrens from Conjuring Franchise (Vera Varmiga & Patrick Wilson) face to face with Liam. There is some suspense like in Non-stop and because the setting in the train, I can't help it to compare with Murder at the Orient Express and yes, beside the glamorous Orient Express rather than NY Metro, this movie has more weight than the other one. For a Neeson-genre, this movie just got score 8/10 from me. A must watch movie for all commuters around jabodetabek just like myself 😹

评论人：fazartheronin
评论时间：2018-01-19
评论内容：Udah nonton THE COMMUTER Dari awal THE COMMUTER emang mau dibikin seperti pendahulunya, NON-STOP (2014). Kedua film ini jadi berasa kembar, tapi ga identik. Yang satu bersetting di kereta, dan satu lagi di pesawat terbang. Secara genre pun sama. Action // Crime //Drama // Mystery // Thriller. Peran utama juga masih Liam Neeson, dan bangku sutradara juga masih dipegang Jaume Collet-Serra. Tapi sayangnya THE COMMUTER menurut gw ga sebagus NON-STOP. Gw lebih suka ketegangan yang disajikan NON-STOP. Gw lebih suka karakter Bill Marks (NON-STOP), ketimbang Michael MacCauley (THE COMMUTER). Gw lebih suka pendalaman semua karakter di NON-STOP. Dan udah pasti gw lebih suka cerita di NON-STOP. Kehadiran duo THE CONJURING (Vera Farmiga & Patrick Wilson) menurut gw belum bisa mengangkat film ini jadi lebih baik, pendalaman karakter mereka masih kurang (mungkin karena durasi mereka tampil sebentar), masih bagus mereka tampil di THE CONJURING. Tapi THE COMMUTER masih layak buat ditonton, terutama yang belum pernah nonton film NON-STOP, ga akan kecewa pastinya, masih enak ditonton & seru nebak-nebak siapa orang yang dicari diantara banyak penumpang. #TheCommuter #NonStop #LiamNeeson #BillMarks #MichaelMacCauley #VeraFarmiga #PatrickWilson

评论内容：Pasażer Premiera Tytuł oryginalny: The Commuter Czas trwania: 104 min. Produkcja: USA , 2017 Gatunek: kryminał / dramat / dreszczowiec Premiera: 12 stycznia 2018 Dystrybutor filmu: Kino Świat Reżyseria: Jaume Collet-Serra Obsada: Vera Farmiga, Liam Neeson, Elizabeth McGovern Bohater kina akcji, Liam Neeson, powraca w trzymającym w napięciu od pierwszej do ostatniej minuty thrillerze w reżyserii mistrza gatunku – Jaume’a Collet-Serra. „Pasażer” – nowe dzieło twórcy przebojów „183 metry strachu” i „Non stop” to pełne gwiazd kino sensacyjne, o szybkości i mocy rozpędzonego pociągu. Historia zwykłego człowieka, uwikłanego w zabójczy spisek, od którego decyzji zależeć będzie życie wielu niewinnych osób. W obsadzie produkcji, obok Neesona, m.in.: Vera Farmiga i Patrick Wilson – niezapomniana para egzorcystów z hitów „Obecność 1 i 2”, Sam Neill („Park Jurajski”) oraz Jonathan Banks, czyli zabójczy Mike Ehrmantraut z kultowych seriali „Zadzwoń do Saula” i „Breaking Bad”. Dla agenta ubezpieczeniowego Michaela Woolricha każdy dzień wygląda tak samo – praca i powrót pociągiem do domu. Wszystko zmienia się, gdy w czasie jednej z podróży poznaje tajemniczą kobietę. Nieznajoma, która wydaje się wiedzieć o Michaelu dosłownie wszystko, zleca mu niezwykłe zadanie. Zanim pociąg dotrze do celu, mężczyzna ma zlokalizować i wskazać osobę, która tego dnia nie powinna się w nim znajdować. Jeśli tego nie zrobi, ucierpi zarówno on sam, jego rodzina, jak i pozostali współpasażerowie. Nie mając wyboru, Michael postanawia rozwiązać zagadkę. Z każdą minutą i przebytym kilometrem stawka rośnie, a mężczyzna przekonuje się, że stał się pionkiem w szalenie niebezpiecznej intrydze. ___ #pomyslnafilm #film #premiera #thecommuter #pasazer

评论人：timc9219
评论时间：2018-01-19
评论内容：The January-February period is often filled with a ton of bad films, which is why it is considered as the 'cinematic wasteland' by established critics, but The Commuter is not one of them. This movie did not bring much new things to the table, but it did hit the right beats in providing a straightforward fun and entertaining action film. First of all, this movie surprisingly had a decent amount of urgency brought about by the fast, breakneck pacing of its story, which was balanced by some great level of suspense throughout. Liam Neeson really carried this movie well by just his mere presence on screen (what do you expect anyway?), and his performance managed to really give the film the tension and 'high stakes situation' feel it needed. The action sequences were also handled neatly and coherently with a ton of great wide shots and nice blend of CGI as well as without a lot of shaky cameras and quick cuts. My only issue with the movie was how it felt too familiar even for the action genre at times, but nevertheless it did not distract from the film much because I had fun with it for the most part. Overall, I would give The Commuter a B. It was certainly not a groundbreaking movie in any way, but it was a pretty good popcorn film that still deserves a checkout for your weekends. #jakarta #liamneeson #vsco #artwork #edit #movie #vscophile #filmmaking #filmphotography #lucasfilms #film #train #2017 #geek #thecommuter #hollywoodstudios #animation #singapore #acting #movies #films #bio #hollywoodmovies #techno #art #tim1912inthemovies #review #hollywood

I do feel that the connection with the main character really just wasn't there, so maybe they should've worked on the character development a little better. Also, the main character's family I had zero connection to at all, deffinetly could use a little backstory with all the characters. But the ending of the film lost me. I feel like it was unnecessary and a little over the top. There were things that just should have been left out of the film completely because they were completely unneeded. 评论人：flyingfilmreviews
评论时间：2018-01-19
评论内容：#TheCommuter (2018): 6/10 ⠀ It’s ten years since Liam Neeson starred in Pierre Morel’s ‘Taken’, and yet, we still can’t seem to get enough of him in that kind of role. Neeson returns in his latest action flick The Commuter, which is pretty much ‘Non-Stop’ meets ‘Murder On The Orient Express’. Michael MacCauley (Neeson) is approached on his way home and seemingly threatened into finding someone on the train. ⠀ There are some nice effects and sweeping shots in the build-up from director Collet-Serra, but in truth we are all ready in waiting for Liam Neeson to spring into action as he so often does. The premise and overall plot are hardly groundbreaking, but the film is still entertaining on the whole. Where ‘Murder On The Orient Express’ attempted sophistication but ended up a little too slow, The Commuter hurtles along at a blistering, uncompromising pace. It’s classic Neeson of the last decade. ⠀ The Commuter will not be winning any awards any time soon, but then we never expected it to. That’s not why people will flock to see it. It’s good old fashioned entertainment. As long as you don’t read too much into the plot itself, such as how MacCauley is able to get away with killing so many people without so much as a ticking off, you’ll have a blast. Get ready for The Commuter, out in UK cinemas on 19th January. ⠀ #FilmReview #MovieReview #Film #Movie #Review #FilmCritic #MovieCritic #Crime #Action #LiamNeeson #VeraFarmiga #PatrickWilson #JonathanBanks #SamNeill #ElizabethMcGovern #KillianScott #ShazadLatif #AndyNyman #ClaraLago #RolandMøller #FlorencePugh #DeanCharlesChapman #EllaRaeSmith #ColinMcFarlane #KobnaHoldbrookSmith #AdamNagaitis #DamsonIdris #JaumeColletSerra

评论内容：《疾速救援》短評 繼《狙擊陌生人》、《空中救援》及《一夜狂奔》後第四次合作，地表最強老爸連恩尼遜和導演豪梅寇勒特斯拉仍交出一部值得一看的B級動作片。 久違動作電影的連恩尼遜也在電影中展現精湛的打鬥技巧，有段令人驚艷幾乎一鏡到底的打鬥畫面格外刺激，血脈噴張。 整體劇情雖公式化，但跟著連恩尼遜一起於列車上揪出兇手懲兇鬥惡依舊爽快。此部有了《厲陰宅》華倫夫婦加入十分驚喜，薇拉法蜜嘉飾演的神秘女子一登場即有戲劇張力，過程中不免一直腦補「瓦拉克」大對抗! 《疾速救援》是部不錯放鬆心情，享受刺激的懸疑推理電影，該有的動作元素皆具備，劇情也不致太差，帶著輕鬆心情，看完會十分舒暢。 給分：6.5/10 #疾速救援 #thecommuter #liamneeson

Sebagai kepala keluarga, ia adalah bapak yang bertanggung jawab. Kemudian Ia sedang mengalami masalah finansial untuk membayar registrasi kuliah anaknya dan mencoba untuk menyelesaikan masalah ini. Kemudian Michael masuk ke kantor dan menemukan bahwa karirnya selama sepuluh tahun sebagai pegawai teladan hilang begitu saja. Ia dipecat dan nasib kuliah anaknya berada di ujung tanduk. Dia bercerita kepada sahabatnya, Murphy (Patrick Wilson), bahwa ia belum berani mengatakan berita ini kepada istrinya. Ia belum tahu bagaimana caranya bertindak. Kemudian Michael masuk ke dalam komuter, transportasi hariannya selama sepuluh tahun terakhir, Ditengah perjalanan, seorang wanita misterius (Vera Farmiga) datang menghampiri dan meminta Michael mengungkap identitas penumpang tersembunyi di dalam kereta api sebelum pemberhentian terakhir. Michael kemudian menyadari sebuah rencana mematikan sedang berlangsung dan ia dijadikan alat dalam sebuah konspirasi kriminal yang dapat yang membahayakan nyawa dirinya dan sesama penumpang dalam kereta api tersebut. 评论人：world.film.stories
评论时间：2018-01-18
评论内容：🌟🌟🌟🌟🌟 The Commuter Part one of the Train Weekend Movie Marathon: Volume 2. I never thought I'd be doing a second Weekend Movie Marathon about trains. Apparently, there is a wide array of films taking place inside or having something to do with trains. Imagine this. You are sixty years old and you take the train to work every single day. The ride is long, yet that gives you enough time to make friends with other passengers. One day, however, you realize that this may be the last time you take the train because you have been fired from your job. Michael (Liam Neeson), an ex-cop, follows that exact routine for the last ten years, until he is fired. On what seems like him last time taking the train back home, Michael is approached by a mysterious woman who introduced herself as Joanna (Vera Farmiga). She makes a very tempting offer to Michael and asks him to do one simple thing: find a person that goes by the name Prynne, who's not a regular in this train. His reward will be twenty-five thousand dollars hidden inside the train and another seventy-five thousand when the job is complete. Michael finds the hidden money, which inadvertently makes him bound to see this request to the end. Being an ex-cop gives Michael the wits and resourcefulness to investigate in a limited amount of time and avoid all obstacles in his way, even the life-threatening ones. In all honesty, I am not a big fan of Liam Neeson. This, however, was a film that offers all that it promises: action, suspense, mystery, and some plot twists. Neither fast nor slow-paced, The Commuter is going to give you an exciting time watching it. 评论内容：The Commuter 7/10 Main cast : Liam Neeson, Vera Farmiga What would happen if Hercule Point is played by Liam Neeson? Well that's what happens in this movie. Yes, the newest Liam Neeson action movie titled "the Commuter" is about an investigation with the added Liam Neeson style of action. Its just like "Nonstop" mixed with "Murder on Orient Express" The story is about a sales property agent that "randomly" meets a woman on the commuter who offers him something tempting. "What if I asked you to do something that would profoundly effect somebody on this train? Someone in this train is doesnt belong. All you have to do is find them" . Yes, that line explains what this movie is all about. From the beginning, the story is well structured. The background of the main character and why he is willing to accept that kind of offer builds with intensity until its climax. Many questions will pop out like "what actually happened?" , " who's the brains behind all of this". These all served greatly neat so "maybe u can't guess correctly". If u dont believe me, try to guess when you watch it. Just forget about logic ... consider this movie as just entertainment and you will enjoy it more because some of the scenes are unlogical and feel very set up but other then that, all great. About the cast, starting with Liam Neeson. He is in his comfort zone playing this kind of role so maybe you will find he's a lil bit boring. And Vera Farmiga, i like her though she doesn't appear much in this movie and feels like the Conjuring reunion because shes play with her "husband" Patrick Wilson. #movie #review #thecommuter #moviegoer #moviefreak #iamwhatiwatch

评论人：iamwhatiwatch
评论时间：2018-01-18
评论内容：The commuter 7/10 Main cast : Liam Neeson, Vera Farmiga Apa yang terjadi kalau hercule point diperankan oleh liam nesson? Well kalian bisa lihat itu di film ini. Yasss... film aksi terbaru liam nesson yang berjudul commuter ini mengangkat tema penyelidikan sebuah kasus atau teka teki dengan bumbu aksi ala liam nesson. Seperti nonton "nonstop" digabung dengan "murder on orient express". Bercerita tentang seorang agen sales properti yang secara "acak" bertemu dengan seorang wanita di sebuah commuter dan ditawari sebuah penawaran yang menggiurkan. "what if i ask you to do something that could performly affect individual on this train, someone on this train is dont belong. All you have to do is find them". Yah... itu adalah Sebuah pertanyaan yang mewakili keseluruhan cerita di film ini. Dari awal cerita dibangun dengan sangat baik, latar belakang tokoh utama dan berbagai alasan sampai ia "mau" melakukan pekerjaan itu dijelaskan terlebih dahulu sehingga membangun ketegangan yang intense sedikit demi sedikan sampai pada klimaksnya dan penonton akan dibuat bertanya tanya dari awal film apa yang terjadi? Siapa dibalik semua ini? Apa latar belakangnya? Dan semua itu semua itu disajikan dengan rapi dan tidak mudah ditebak. Kalau tidak percaya, coba kalian nonton dan tebaklah. Lupakan soal logika... anggap aja ini sebuah hiburan dan jika kalian melakukan itu kalian akan menikmati film ini karena ada beberapa adegan yang diluar akal sehat dan Terlalu banyak kebetulan seperti semua sudah diskenario. Tapi terlepas dari itu, film ini sangat menarik. Semua cast disini bermain dengan sangat baik dan memang tampaknya liam nesson belum bisa beranjak dari peran peran di zona nyamannya, sehinggal terasa sedikit membosankan. Lihat saja seperti "nonstop", atau "taken". Vera Farmiga bermain baik walau cuma muncul sedikit dan disini dia beradu akting lagi dengan "suaminya" patrick wilson. #movie #moviegoer #review #thecommuter

评论人：movietime_with_craig
评论时间：2018-01-18
评论内容：• C • The first 2/3 of this movie are awesome and fun - and then the last 3rd goes completely off the rails. The premise is genius: a man gets on his normal train home from work (after getting fired) and is told by a woman he'll get $100K if he finds the one person on the train who doesn't belong. I usually love thrillers with simple plots like this - and for a while it works. And then the last 30 minutes or so requires full abandonment of belief and physics and makes absolutely zero sense (also it's painfully obvious who the villain is from the beginning). Such a bummer because the initial idea is intense and intriguing - and then it all falls apart. I love Liam Neeson but this was clearly just a paycheck. #thecommuter #liamneeson

Dans ce film, Liam Neeson nous transporte dans les aventures d’un ex flic qui voit sa vie monotone et répétitive, chamboulée par l’arrivée d’un femme qui va lui proposer un dilemme où l’argent fait vaciller la morale. Entre Speed de Keanu Reeves et 13 block de Bruce Willis, on retrouve dans ce film un personnage principal charismatique, tiraillé entre le bien et le mal, et dont la vie n’a pas toujours été rose. Un scénario plein d’énigmes où on ne sait jamais ce qui va arriver et un tempo entre action et suspens soutenu jusqu’à la fin du film. À voir, vous ne serez pas déçu! 评论内容：As usual I didn't watch the trailer for this movie, I don't like watching trailers for movies because I want the movie going experience to be a suprise. I only saw the poster before going into the movie, there was a statement that stated "from the director of Non-Stop and The Shallows". To summarize this movie, This movie was basically Non-Stop all over again except this time it's Liam Neeson on a train. I could see someone enjoying this movie if they haven't seen Non-Stop but for me it was so predictable from start to finish. There are some ridiculously implausible scenes that would fit perfectly in a Fast and Furious movie. I did find some parts of this movie to be enjoyable at times, like Liam Neeson kicking ass despite constantly feeling like it's a rethread of Non-Stop and a number of other movies. As far as January movies go it's decent entertainment.

Film yang dibintangi oleh Liam Neeson dan Vera Farmiga ini menurut gw cukup memberikan banyak pertanyaan di benak gw yang perlahan terbangun dari awal Michael naik kereta. Michael ini termasuk penumpang yang menurut gw cukup kepo dengan urusan penumpang lain. Sehingga dia bisa hafal siapa saja orang yang naik kereta barengan dengan dia di jam yang sama selama 10 tahun terakhir. Semakin berumur, Liam Neeson makin sering memainkan peran sebagai bapak bijak dan baik juga kepala keluarga yang tangguh. Gw suka semangatnya di film ini. ★★★ #thecommuter

评论内容：NEW EPISODE! (Listen / download) That Film Stew Ep 103 - The Commuter Review (LINK IN BIO) The action thriller The Commuter is directed by Jaume Collet-Serra, and stars Liam Neeson, Vera Farmiga, Patrick Wilson, Jonathan Banks, Elizabeth McGovern, and Sam Neil. Thanks to Anarchy PR (@anarchy_pr), we were given to opportunity to attend an advanced screening of the film. Michael McCauley (played by Liam Neeson), is an ex-cop, now insurance salesman, who is on his daily commute home – taking the metro train. A mysterious stranger (played by Vera Farmiga), offers him $100,000 if he identifies a hidden passenger on his train before the last stop. As he works against the clock to solve the puzzle, he realises he is caught in midst of a deadly criminal conspiracy and that his life and the lives of his fellow passengers are at risk. Does The Commuter manage to stay on track or does the movie get derailed before the credits roll? Check out what we thought in our review (we manage to keep it relatively spoiler-free until about the 10 minute mark). The Commuter opens officially in Australia on Thursday 18th January 2018.
